+/**
+ * Client controller for the `/dev/pipelines` studio page (Phase 6
+ * Task 6.4).
+ *
+ * Responsibilities:
+ *
+ *   1. **Live command preview.** Every form (the New form + each
+ *      template's Edit panel's five sub-operations) carries one
+ *      `<code data-pipelines-preview="<scope>">` element. The
+ *      controller rebuilds the preview on every change event so the
+ *      operator sees the assembled slash command before clicking
+ *      Copy.
+ *
+ *   2. **Clipboard copy.** Every copy button (`[data-pipelines-copy-
+ *      button="<scope>"]` on forms, `[data-pipeline-copy]` on table
+ *      rows for the Delete affordance) clipboards its payload through
+ *      `copyOrShowFallback` and flashes a "Copied" affirmation.
+ *
+ *   3. **Per-row View / Edit toggles (single-open accordion).** A
+ *      single module-level tracker holds the currently-open panel id
+ *      across View and Edit — opening a new View or Edit auto-closes
+ *      whichever was previously open. View and Edit are mutually
+ *      exclusive per row too: opening Edit on row R closes Row R's
+ *      View if it was open, and vice versa.
+ *
+ *   4. **Edit sub-operation single-open accordion.** Inside one Edit
+ *      panel, the five `<details data-pipelines-op>` panels behave
+ *      as a single-open accordion: opening one closes the others.
+ *      This mirrors the CLI's mutually-exclusive contract — only
+ *      one update operation runs per invocation.
+ *
+ * Slash-command quoting: every operator-supplied value flows through
+ * `quoteValue()` (JSON.stringify). The CLI accepts the resulting
+ * double-quoted, backslash-escaped form for every flag.
+ *
+ * Idempotent: when the page has no `[data-pipelines-container]`,
+ * init is a no-op. The lanes-page controller's bundle shares the same
+ * surface; both inits run on every page and short-circuit when their
+ * markers are absent.
+ *
+ * THESIS Consequence 2: the controller never mutates state on the
+ * server. There are no fetch / POST paths; every operator action
+ * resolves to a clipboard write + paste in Claude Code.
+ */
+
+import { copyAndFlash } from '../copy-builder.ts';
+
+/**
+ * Quote an operator-supplied value for inclusion in a slash command.
+ * `JSON.stringify` wraps in double quotes and escapes embedded quotes,
+ * backslashes, and control characters — applied symmetrically across
+ * id / shape / name / description / stage names so injection-shape
+ * inputs can't slip through if pasted into a shell.
+ */
+function quoteValue(value: string): string {
+  return JSON.stringify(value);
+}
+
+/**
+ * Module-level tracker for the currently-open per-row panel (View or
+ * Edit). Each entry is `{ pipelineId, panel: 'view'|'edit' }`. Used
+ * by the single-open accordion logic so opening any panel auto-closes
+ * the previously-open one (cross-row AND cross-panel).
+ */
+interface OpenPanelState {
+  readonly pipelineId: string;
+  readonly panel: 'view' | 'edit';
+}
+
+let openPanel: OpenPanelState | null = null;
+
+/**
+ * Read a field's trimmed value from a form. Returns empty string when
+ * the field is absent so callers can treat "missing" and "blank" as
+ * equivalent for the preview-rebuild path.
+ */
+function readField(form: HTMLElement, name: string): string {
+  const el = form.querySelector<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>(
+    `[data-pipelines-field="${name}"]`,
+  );
+  return el?.value.trim() ?? '';
+}
+
+/**
+ * Read a set of checkbox values (used by the set-locked sub-operation).
+ * Returns the values of every checked input in document order.
+ */
+function readCheckedValues(form: HTMLElement, name: string): string[] {
+  const els = Array.from(
+    form.querySelectorAll<HTMLInputElement>(
+      `input[type="checkbox"][data-pipelines-field="${name}"]`,
+    ),
+  );
+  return els.filter((el) => el.checked).map((el) => el.value);
+}
+
+/** Build the `/deskwork:pipeline create` command from the New form. */
+function buildCreateCommand(form: HTMLElement): string {
+  const id = readField(form, 'new-id');
+  const shape = readField(form, 'new-shape');
+  const name = readField(form, 'new-name');
+  const description = readField(form, 'new-description');
+
+  const idArg = id.length > 0 ? quoteValue(id) : '<id>';
+  const shapeArg = shape.length > 0 ? quoteValue(shape) : '<stages>';
+  const nameFragment = name.length > 0 ? ` --name ${quoteValue(name)}` : '';
+  const descFragment =
+    description.length > 0 ? ` --description ${quoteValue(description)}` : '';
+  return `/deskwork:pipeline create ${idArg} --shape ${shapeArg}${nameFragment}${descFragment}`;
+}
+
+function rebuildNewPreview(form: HTMLElement): string {
+  const command = buildCreateCommand(form);
+  const preview = form.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
+    '[data-pipelines-preview="new"]',
+  );
+  if (preview) preview.textContent = command;
+  return command;
+}
+
+/** Build the `/deskwork:pipeline update <id> --add-stage ...` command. */
+function buildAddCommand(form: HTMLElement, pipelineId: string): string {
+  const name = readField(form, 'add-name');
+  const position = readField(form, 'add-position');
+  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
+  const nameArg = name.length > 0 ? quoteValue(name) : '<name>';
+  const positionFragment =
+    position.length > 0 ? ` --position ${position}` : '';
+  return `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --add-stage ${nameArg}${positionFragment}`;
+}
+
+/** Build the `--rename-stage <from> --to-stage <to>` command. */
+function buildRenameCommand(form: HTMLElement, pipelineId: string): string {
+  const from = readField(form, 'rename-from');
+  const to = readField(form, 'rename-to');
+  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
+  const fromArg = from.length > 0 ? quoteValue(from) : '<from>';
+  const toArg = to.length > 0 ? quoteValue(to) : '<to>';
+  return `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --rename-stage ${fromArg} --to-stage ${toArg}`;
+}
+
+/** Build the `--remove-stage <name>` command. */
+function buildRemoveCommand(form: HTMLElement, pipelineId: string): string {
+  const name = readField(form, 'remove-name');
+  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
+  const nameArg = name.length > 0 ? quoteValue(name) : '<name>';
+  return `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --remove-stage ${nameArg}`;
+}
+
+/** Build the `--set-locked "s1,s2,..."` command. */
+function buildSetLockedCommand(form: HTMLElement, pipelineId: string): string {
+  const checked = readCheckedValues(form, 'set-locked');
+  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
+  const csv = checked.join(',');
+  // Empty selection means "clear all locks" — emit `--set-locked ""`
+  // so the CLI sees an explicit empty list rather than an absent flag.
+  return `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --set-locked ${quoteValue(csv)}`;
+}
+
+/** Build the `--set-off-pipeline "s1,s2,..."` command. */
+function buildSetOffCommand(form: HTMLElement, pipelineId: string): string {
+  const csv = readField(form, 'set-off-pipeline');
+  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
+  return `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --set-off-pipeline ${quoteValue(csv)}`;
+}
+
+type UpdateOp =
+  | 'add'
+  | 'rename'
+  | 'remove'
+  | 'set-locked'
+  | 'set-off-pipeline';
+
+function rebuildEditPreview(
+  form: HTMLElement,
+  op: UpdateOp,
+  pipelineId: string,
+): string {
+  let command: string;
+  switch (op) {
+    case 'add':
+      command = buildAddCommand(form, pipelineId);
+      break;
+    case 'rename':
+      command = buildRenameCommand(form, pipelineId);
+      break;
+    case 'remove':
+      command = buildRemoveCommand(form, pipelineId);
+      break;
+    case 'set-locked':
+      command = buildSetLockedCommand(form, pipelineId);
+      break;
+    case 'set-off-pipeline':
+      command = buildSetOffCommand(form, pipelineId);
+      break;
+  }
+  const preview = form.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
+    `[data-pipelines-preview="${op}"]`,
+  );
+  if (preview) preview.textContent = command;
+  return command;
+}
+
+function initNewForm(container: HTMLElement): void {
+  const form = container.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-pipelines-new-form]');
+  if (!form) return;
+  const inputs = Array.from(
+    form.querySelectorAll<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>(
+      '[data-pipelines-field]',
+    ),
+  );
+  const rebuild = (): void => {
+    rebuildNewPreview(form);
+  };
+  for (const input of inputs) {
+    input.addEventListener('input', rebuild);
+    input.addEventListener('change', rebuild);
+  }
+  rebuild();
+
+  const copy = form.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
+    '[data-pipelines-copy-button="new"]',
+  );
+  if (copy) {
+    copy.addEventListener('click', async () => {
+      const command = rebuildNewPreview(form);
+      await copyAndFlash(command, copy, 'Copied create command');
+    });
+  }
+}
+
+const UPDATE_OPS: readonly UpdateOp[] = [
+  'add',
+  'rename',
+  'remove',
+  'set-locked',
+  'set-off-pipeline',
+];
+
+function initEditOpForm(
+  panel: HTMLElement,
+  op: UpdateOp,
+  pipelineId: string,
+): void {
+  const form = panel.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
+    `[data-pipelines-op-form="${op}"]`,
+  );
+  if (!form) return;
+  const inputs = Array.from(
+    form.querySelectorAll<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>(
+      '[data-pipelines-field]',
+    ),
+  );
+  const rebuild = (): void => {
+    rebuildEditPreview(form, op, pipelineId);
+  };
+  for (const input of inputs) {
+    input.addEventListener('input', rebuild);
+    input.addEventListener('change', rebuild);
+  }
+  rebuild();
+
+  const copy = form.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
+    `[data-pipelines-copy-button="${op}"]`,
+  );
+  if (copy) {
+    copy.addEventListener('click', async () => {
+      const command = rebuildEditPreview(form, op, pipelineId);
+      await copyAndFlash(command, copy, `Copied ${op} command`);
+    });
+  }
+}
+
+/**
+ * Wire the single-open accordion across the five `<details
+ * data-pipelines-op>` sub-panels inside one Edit panel. Opening any
+ * one closes the others — matches the CLI's mutually-exclusive
+ * contract.
+ */
+function initEditSubAccordion(panel: HTMLElement): void {
+  const details = Array.from(
+    panel.querySelectorAll<HTMLDetailsElement>('[data-pipelines-op]'),
+  );
+  for (const target of details) {
+    target.addEventListener('toggle', () => {
+      if (!target.open) return;
+      for (const other of details) {
+        if (other !== target && other.open) other.open = false;
+      }
+    });
+  }
+}
+
+function initEditPanels(container: HTMLElement): void {
+  const panels = Array.from(
+    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('[data-pipelines-edit-panel]'),
+  );
+  for (const panel of panels) {
+    const pipelineId = panel.dataset.pipelineId;
+    if (!pipelineId) continue;
+    for (const op of UPDATE_OPS) {
+      initEditOpForm(panel, op, pipelineId);
+    }
+    initEditSubAccordion(panel);
+  }
+}
+
+/**
+ * Close a hidden panel row (View or Edit) and reset its toggle's
+ * aria-expanded. Used by the single-open accordion when a sibling
+ * panel opens.
+ */
+function closePanelRow(
+  container: HTMLElement,
+  pipelineId: string,
+  panel: 'view' | 'edit',
+): void {
+  const rowSelector =
+    panel === 'view' ? 'data-pipeline-view-row' : 'data-pipeline-edit-row';
+  const toggleSelector =
+    panel === 'view' ? 'data-pipeline-view-toggle' : 'data-pipeline-edit-toggle';
+  const row = container.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
+    `[${rowSelector}][data-pipeline-id="${pipelineId}"]`,
+  );
+  const toggle = container.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
+    `[${toggleSelector}][data-pipeline-id="${pipelineId}"]`,
+  );
+  if (row) row.hidden = true;
+  if (toggle) toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
+}
+
+function initRowToggles(container: HTMLElement): void {
+  const wire = (panel: 'view' | 'edit', toggleAttr: string, rowAttr: string): void => {
+    const toggles = Array.from(
+      container.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(`[${toggleAttr}]`),
+    );
+    for (const toggle of toggles) {
+      const pipelineId = toggle.dataset.pipelineId;
+      if (!pipelineId) continue;
+      toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
+        const target = container.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
+          `[${rowAttr}][data-pipeline-id="${pipelineId}"]`,
+        );
+        if (!target) return;
+        const willOpen = target.hidden;
+        if (willOpen && openPanel !== null) {
+          // Close whichever panel was previously open (could be the
+          // same row's sibling panel or a different row's panel).
+          closePanelRow(container, openPanel.pipelineId, openPanel.panel);
+        }
+        target.hidden = !willOpen;
+        toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(willOpen));
+        openPanel = willOpen ? { pipelineId, panel } : null;
+      });
+    }
+  };
+  wire('view', 'data-pipeline-view-toggle', 'data-pipeline-view-row');
+  wire('edit', 'data-pipeline-edit-toggle', 'data-pipeline-edit-row');
+
+  const cancels = Array.from(
+    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>('[data-pipeline-edit-cancel]'),
+  );
+  for (const cancel of cancels) {
+    const pipelineId = cancel.dataset.pipelineId;
+    if (!pipelineId) continue;
+    cancel.addEventListener('click', () => {
+      closePanelRow(container, pipelineId, 'edit');
+      if (openPanel?.pipelineId === pipelineId && openPanel.panel === 'edit') {
+        openPanel = null;
+      }
+    });
+  }
+}
+
+function initRowCopyButtons(container: HTMLElement): void {
+  const buttons = Array.from(
+    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>('[data-pipeline-copy]'),
+  );
+  for (const button of buttons) {
+    button.addEventListener('click', async () => {
+      const command = button.dataset.copy;
+      if (!command || command.length === 0) return;
+      await copyAndFlash(command, button, `Copied ${command}`);
+    });
+  }
+}
+
+/**
+ * Wire every interactive control on the pipelines page. Idempotent —
+ * absent `[data-pipelines-container]` short-circuits, so importing
+ * this from a shared bundle on other surfaces is harmless.
+ */
+export function initPipelinesPage(): void {
+  // Reset module-level state so repeat init calls (e.g. across tests)
+  // don't carry a stale open-panel tracker.
+  openPanel = null;
+  const container = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
+    '[data-pipelines-container]',
+  );
+  if (!container) return;
+  initNewForm(container);
+  initEditPanels(container);
+  initRowToggles(container);
+  initRowCopyButtons(container);
+}


## What to look for

- **Correctness bugs** — logic errors, off-by-one, null/undefined paths, race conditions, missing error handling, swallowed exceptions.
- **Design issues** — coupling between layers that should be independent, leaking abstractions, primitives that should compose but don't, configuration that should be data ending up as code.
- **Missed edge cases** — what happens with empty input? Maximum input? Concurrent calls? Partial failure? Network unavailability? Operator interrupt mid-operation? What is the behavior on a fresh install vs. an upgrade?
- **Code-quality concerns** — files growing past a reasonable cap, names that don't reveal intent, dead code, duplicated logic, magic numbers without explanation, tests that don't test the contract they claim to test.
- **Cross-cutting impact** — does this diff touch a surface that other surfaces depend on? Are those other surfaces updated? Are migrations needed? Are doctor rules / schemas / validators updated to match the new shape?
- **Documentation drift** — does the README / SKILL.md / PRD describe the behavior the code actually implements? If the spec changed, did the implementation? If the implementation changed, did the spec?
- **Operator-discipline traps** — placeholder comments, swallowed errors, hardcoded paths/values that should be configurable, fallbacks that hide failure modes, mock data outside test code. These are bug-factories per project guidelines.

## Output format

For each finding you surface, emit ONE markdown block in this exact shape:

```
### <heading: one-line summary of the finding>

Finding-ID: AUDIT-BARRAGE-<your-model-name>-<NN>
Status:     open
Severity:   <blocking | high | medium | low | informational>
Surface:    <repo-relative-path:line-range> OR <description of the surface if not anchored to a single file>

<one-to-three paragraphs of body: what the finding is, why it matters, what evidence you relied on, what a reasonable fix would look like. Be specific. Cite line numbers from the diff. If the finding is structural / cross-file, name every file affected.>
```

Number the findings sequentially (`-01`, `-02`, ...). Use `blocking` only for issues that would break the feature's stated goals in obvious ways; `high` for correctness bugs adopters will hit; `medium` for design issues that compound over time; `low` for hygiene; `informational` for context you think the operator should see but isn't itself a bug.

## If you find nothing — say so explicitly

If you walk the diff carefully and find no findings worth surfacing, emit ONE block in this shape instead:

```
### No findings

Finding-ID: AUDIT-BARRAGE-<your-model-name>-CLEAN
Status:     open
Severity:   informational
Surface:    (the entire diff)

I walked the diff for the feature named above and found no findings worth surfacing. My specific reasoning: <three-to-five sentences explaining what you checked, why those checks came back clean, and what you would have flagged if it had been present.>
```

**Do not pad with weak findings.** A confident "I checked X, Y, Z and they are clean for these reasons" is more useful to the operator than three vague low-severity notes. The cross-model diversity gives the operator independent signal; an empty clean report from your CLI is itself a signal when paired with findings from your siblings.

## Hard constraints

- **No deferral phrases.** Don't write phrases like "fix later", "address in a follow-up", or other commitments to deferred work. The dispatch-wrapper rejects these as bug-factories. If you spot a deferral phrase IN the diff, surface it as a finding.
- **Anchor findings to evidence.** A finding that says "this might be a problem" without naming the specific file + line is not actionable. Name the surface, quote the relevant code, explain what's wrong.
- **One issue per finding block.** Don't bundle multiple concerns into one entry; the operator triages each block as a discrete signal.
- **Provenance is your model name.** Replace `<your-model-name>` in the Finding-ID with the CLI you are (`claude`, `codex`, `gemini`, etc.). This is how the operator joins findings across models.

codex
I’ll audit this as a review pass and keep it to concrete, triageable findings anchored in the diff. I’m going to inspect the touched renderer/client files directly so the line references match the working tree.

   110	function renderDeleteButton(row: PipelineRow): RawHtml {
   111	  // Two gates surface as visibly-disabled chrome so the operator sees
   112	  // the obstruction before clicking. The CLI enforces the same gates;
   113	  // these are the visual mirrors.

   122	      >${COPY_BTN_DELETE_LABEL}</button>`);
   123	  }
   124	  if (row.referencingLanes.length > 0) {
   125	    const noun = row.referencingLanes.length === 1 ? 'lane' : 'lanes';
   126	    const list = row.referencingLanes.join(', ');
   127	    return unsafe(html`
   128	      <div class="pipelines-delete-blocked" data-pipelines-delete-blocked>
   129	        <button
   130	          class="pipelines-btn pipelines-btn--delete-disabled"
   131	          type="button"
   132	          disabled
   133	          aria-disabled="true"
   134	          aria-describedby="pipelines-delete-deps-${row.id}"
   135	          title="Cannot delete: ${row.referencingLanes.length} ${noun} reference this template (${list}). Reassign first via /deskwork:pipeline delete ${row.id} --reassign-lanes-to <other-id>."
   136	        >${COPY_BTN_DELETE_LABEL} — ${row.referencingLanes.length} ${noun}</button>
   137	        <p class="pipelines-delete-deps" id="pipelines-delete-deps-${row.id}" data-pipelines-delete-deps>
   138	          Used by <code>${list}</code>. Reassign via
   139	          <code>/deskwork:pipeline delete ${row.id} --reassign-lanes-to &lt;other-id&gt;</code>.
   140	        </p>
   141	      </div>`);
   142	  }
   143	  return unsafe(html`
   144	    <button
   145	      class="pipelines-btn pipelines-btn--delete"
   146	      type="button"
   147	      data-pipeline-copy
   148	      data-copy="/deskwork:pipeline delete ${row.id}"
   149	      title="Copy /deskwork:pipeline delete ${row.id} to clipboard"
   150	    >${COPY_BTN_DELETE_LABEL}</button>`);
   151	}
   152	
   153	function describeErrorKind(kind: PipelineLoadErrorKind): string {
   154	  switch (kind) {
   155	    case 'parse':
   156	      return 'JSON parse error';
   157	    case 'zod':
   158	      return 'Schema validation failed';
   159	    case 'id-mismatch':
   160	      return 'id field disagrees with filename basename';
   161	    case 'missing':
   162	      return 'File not found';
   163	    case 'unknown':
   164	      return 'Load error';
   165	  }
   166	}
   167	
   168	function renderErrorRow(row: PipelineErrorRow): RawHtml {
   169	  const noun = row.referencingLanes.length === 1 ? 'lane' : 'lanes';
   170	  const dependents =
   171	    row.referencingLanes.length > 0
   172	      ? html`<p class="pipelines-error-dependents">${row.referencingLanes.length} ${noun} reference this template: <code>${row.referencingLanes.join(', ')}</code></p>`
   173	      : '';
   174	
   175	  return unsafe(html`
   176	    <tr class="pipelines-row pipelines-row--error" data-pipeline-row data-pipeline-id="${row.id}" data-pipeline-error>
   177	      <td class="pipelines-cell pipelines-cell--id"><code>${row.id}</code></td>
   178	      <td class="pipelines-cell pipelines-cell--source">
   179	        <span class="pipelines-source pipelines-source--error" title="Template failed to load">error</span>
   180	      </td>
   181	      <td class="pipelines-cell" colspan="5">
   182	        <div class="pipelines-error" data-pipeline-error-detail>
   183	          <p class="pipelines-error-kind">${describeErrorKind(row.error.kind)}</p>
   184	          <p class="pipelines-error-path">at <code>${row.error.path}</code></p>
   185	          <pre class="pipelines-error-message">${row.error.message}</pre>
   186	          ${unsafe(dependents)}
   187	        </div>
   188	      </td>
   189	    </tr>`);
   190	}
   191

   205	export function renderPipelineTable(input: RenderPipelineTableInput): RawHtml {

   227	      <tbody>

   229	        ${input.errors.map((row) => renderErrorRow(row))}
   230	      </tbody>

    35	interface RenderLaneTableInput {
    36	  readonly rows: readonly LaneRow[];
    37	  readonly availableTemplates: readonly string[];
    38	  readonly emptyMessage: string;

    43	
    44	function renderTableRow(
    45	  row: LaneRow,
    46	  availableTemplates: readonly string[],
    47	): RawHtml {
    48	  const archiveOrRestore = row.archived
    49	    ? renderCopyButton({
    50	        label: COPY_BTN_RESTORE_LABEL,
    51	        copy: `/deskwork:lane restore ${row.id}`,
    52	        variant: 'restore',
    53	      })
    54	    : renderCopyButton({
    55	        label: COPY_BTN_ARCHIVE_LABEL,
    56	        copy: `/deskwork:lane archive ${row.id}`,
    57	        variant: 'archive',
    58	      });
    59	
    60	  // Purge is gated to archived + zero-entry rows. The CLI enforces
    61	  // the gate too; the page surfaces it visually to reduce the chance
    62	  // the operator runs a refused command.
    63	  //
    64	  // When the lane is archived but still has entries, render a
    65	  // visibly-disabled Purge button that names the gate ("N entries")
    66	  // and explains the next step in its title. The disabled state
    67	  // makes the gate discoverable — without it, the operator sees no
    68	  // affordance at all and stalls.
    69	  let purgeButton: RawHtml | '' = '';
    70	  if (row.archived && row.entryCount === 0) {
    71	    purgeButton = renderCopyButton({
    72	      label: COPY_BTN_PURGE_LABEL,
    73	      copy: `/deskwork:lane purge ${row.id}`,
    74	      variant: 'purge',
    75	    });
    76	  } else if (row.archived && row.entryCount > 0) {
    77	    purgeButton = renderDisabledPurgeButton(row.entryCount);
    78	  }
    79	
    80	  return unsafe(html`
    81	    <tr class="lanes-row" data-lane-row data-lane-id="${row.id}"${unsafe(row.archived ? ' data-archived' : '')}>
    82	      <td class="lanes-cell lanes-cell--handle">
    83	        <span
    84	          class="lanes-reorder-handle"
    85	          aria-hidden="true"
    86	          title="Reorder via the dashboard lane rail"
    87	        >⋮</span>
    88	      </td>
    89	      <td class="lanes-cell lanes-cell--id"><code>${row.id}</code></td>
    90	      <td class="lanes-cell lanes-cell--name">${row.name}</td>
    91	      <td class="lanes-cell lanes-cell--template"><code>${row.pipelineTemplate}</code></td>
    92	      <td class="lanes-cell lanes-cell--content-dir"><code>${row.contentDir}</code></td>
    93	      <td class="lanes-cell lanes-cell--count">${row.entryCount}</td>
    94	      <td class="lanes-cell lanes-cell--visibility">
    95	        <span
    96	          class="lanes-visibility-icon"
    97	          aria-label="${row.archived ? 'Archived' : 'Visible'}"
    98	          title="${row.archived ? 'Archived — hidden by default in the dashboard.' : 'Visible in the dashboard (operator may flip per-operator visibility client-side).'}"
    99	        >${row.archived ? '◌' : '◉'}</span>
   100	      </td>
   101	      <td class="lanes-cell lanes-cell--actions">
   102	        <button
   103	          class="lanes-btn lanes-btn--edit"
   104	          type="button"
   105	          data-lane-edit-toggle
   106	          data-lane-id="${row.id}"
   107	          aria-expanded="false"

   109	        >${COPY_BTN_EDIT_LABEL}</button>

   113	    </tr>
   114	    <tr class="lanes-row lanes-row--edit-form" data-lane-edit-row data-lane-id="${row.id}" hidden>
   115	      <td class="lanes-cell" colspan="8">
   116	        ${renderEditForm(row, availableTemplates)}
   117	      </td>
   118	    </tr>`);
   119	}
   120	
   121	interface CopyButtonInput {
   122	  readonly label: string;
   123	  readonly copy: string;
   124	  readonly variant: 'archive' | 'restore' | 'purge';
   125	}
   126

   141	 * (move entries first) discoverable; the title explains the next

   152	      disabled
   153	      aria-disabled="true"
   154	      title="Cannot purge: ${entryCount} ${noun} still reference this lane. Move them to another lane first via the per-entry surface."
   155	    >${COPY_BTN_PURGE_LABEL} — ${entryCount} ${noun}</button>`);

   158	/**
   159	 * Render a lane table with caption + thead + tbody. Empty rows fall
   160	 * back to the supplied empty-message inside a single colspan cell so
   161	 * the table chrome is still visible (per DESIGN-STANDARDS structure-
   162	 * over-scrolling — even an empty hierarchy node communicates the
   163	 * shape of the page).
   164	 */
   165	export function renderLaneTable(input: RenderLaneTableInput): RawHtml {
   166	  if (input.rows.length === 0) {
   167	    return unsafe(html`
   168	      <table
   169	        class="lanes-table${unsafe(input.archivedTable ? ' lanes-table--archived' : '')}"
   170	        data-lanes-table${unsafe(input.archivedTable ? ' data-archived' : '')}
   171	      >
   172	        <caption class="lanes-table-caption">${input.tableLabel}</caption>
   173	        <thead>${renderHeadRow()}</thead>
   174	        <tbody>
   175	          <tr class="lanes-row lanes-row--empty">
   176	            <td class="lanes-cell lanes-cell--empty" colspan="8">${input.emptyMessage}</td>
   177	          </tr>
   178	        </tbody>
   179	      </table>`);
   180	  }
   181	  return unsafe(html`
   182	    <table
   183	      class="lanes-table${unsafe(input.archivedTable ? ' lanes-table--archived' : '')}"
   184	      data-lanes-table${unsafe(input.archivedTable ? ' data-archived' : '')}
   185	    >
   186	      <caption class="lanes-table-caption">${input.tableLabel}</caption>
   187	      <thead>${renderHeadRow()}</thead>
   188	      <tbody>
   189	        ${input.rows.map((row) => renderTableRow(row, input.availableTemplates))}
   190	      </tbody>
   191	    </table>`);
   192	}
   193	
   194	function renderHeadRow(): RawHtml {
   195	  return unsafe(html`
   196	    <tr>
   197	      <th class="lanes-th lanes-th--handle" scope="col" aria-label="Reorder handle"></th>

   201	      <th class="lanes-th lanes-th--content-dir" scope="col">Content dir</th>
   202	      <th class="lanes-th lanes-th--count" scope="col">Entries</th>
   203	      <th class="lanes-th lanes-th--visibility" scope="col">State</th>
   204	      <th class="lanes-th lanes-th--actions" scope="col">Actions</th>
   205	    </tr>`);
   206	}

     1	/**
     2	 * Data layer for the `/dev/pipelines` studio page (Phase 6 Task 6.4).
     3	 *
     4	 * Enumerates every pipeline template visible to the project — the
     5	 * union of plugin-shipped presets and operator-authored project
     6	 * overrides — and joins per-template metadata the page needs to
     7	 * render: source (`plugin-preset` vs `project-override`), the resolved
     8	 * template (linearStages / lockedStages / offPipelineStages), and the
     9	 * number of active+archived lanes that reference each template id.
    10	 *
    11	 * Per the Phase 2 follow-up captured in the workplan (Task 6.4 lead-in
    12	 * note), `listAvailablePipelineTemplates` returns id strings without
    13	 * pre-validating each template. A malformed
    14	 * `<projectRoot>/.deskwork/pipelines/<id>.json` (parse error, Zod
    15	 * violation, id-mismatch) appears in the picker but fails when the
    16	 * page tries to load it. The data layer surfaces such failures as
    17	 * `PipelineLoadError` rows so the renderer can show them inline —
    18	 * "this id exists but won't load — fix it" rather than silently
    19	 * filtering the id out and making the malformation invisible.
    20	 *
    21	 * The same posture as the lanes data layer: read-only, no fallbacks,
    22	 * one pass through disk per page render. No caching — the page is a
    23	 * cold-path operator surface.
    24	 */
    25	
    26	import { existsSync, readFileSync } from 'node:fs';
    27	import { join } from 'node:path';
    28	import {
    29	  listAvailablePipelineTemplates,
    30	  loadPipelineTemplate,
    31	  isPluginPresetPipeline,
    32	  hasPipelineOverride,
    33	  pipelineOverridePath,
    34	  pipelinePluginDefaultPath,
    35	  type PipelineTemplate,
    36	} from '@deskwork/core/pipelines';
    37	import { listLaneConfigs } from '@deskwork/core/lanes';
    38	
    39	/**
    40	 * Where a template's authoritative JSON came from. A template that
    41	 * has BOTH an override and a plugin preset is reported as
    42	 * `project-override` (override-takes-precedence; the loader resolves
    43	 * the override first).
    44	 */
    45	export type PipelineSource = 'plugin-preset' | 'project-override';
    46	
    47	/**
    48	 * Why a template failed to load when the loader was invoked. Surfaced
    49	 * by the data layer so the renderer can show the operator a row with
    50	 * an actionable next step (fix the JSON; mismatched id; missing file).
    51	 *
    52	 * `parse` — JSON.parse threw.
    53	 * `zod` — schema validation rejected the parsed value.
    54	 * `id-mismatch` — JSON's `id` field disagrees with the filename basename.
    55	 * `missing` — file did not exist (should not happen for ids returned
    56	 *   by the enumerator; included for completeness).
    57	 * `unknown` — any other Error shape; the underlying message is
    58	 *   preserved verbatim so the operator can see what the loader said.
    59	 */
    60	export type PipelineLoadErrorKind =
    61	  | 'parse'
    62	  | 'zod'
    63	  | 'id-mismatch'
    64	  | 'missing'
    65	  | 'unknown';
    66	
    67	/**
    68	 * Per-template load-error record. The renderer maps these to error
    69	 * rows in the table; the `path` names the file on disk the operator
    70	 * should open, and `message` is the loader's verbatim diagnostic.
    71	 */
    72	export interface PipelineLoadError {
    73	  readonly kind: PipelineLoadErrorKind;
    74	  readonly path: string;
    75	  readonly message: string;
    76	}
    77	
    78	/**
    79	 * Per-template summary surfaced to the renderer for a healthy
    80	 * (loadable) template.
    81	 */
    82	export interface PipelineRow {
    83	  readonly id: string;
    84	  readonly source: PipelineSource;
    85	  readonly name: string;
    86	  readonly description: string;
    87	  readonly linearStages: readonly string[];
    88	  readonly lockedStages: readonly string[];
    89	  readonly offPipelineStages: readonly string[];
    90	  /**
    91	   * Active + archived lanes whose `pipelineTemplate` equals this id.
    92	   * Used by the renderer to gate Delete and surface dependents in the
    93	   * disabled-state tooltip.
    94	   */
    95	  readonly referencingLanes: readonly string[];
    96	}
    97	
    98	/**
    99	 * Per-template error record (template id appeared in the enumerator
   100	 * but failed to load).
   101	 */
   102	export interface PipelineErrorRow {
   103	  readonly id: string;
   104	  readonly source: PipelineSource;
   105	  readonly error: PipelineLoadError;
   106	  /**
   107	   * Lanes that reference this id, computed against the id-string only
   108	   * (no template load needed). Surfaced so the operator sees who
   109	   * depends on this broken template.
   110	   */
   111	  readonly referencingLanes: readonly string[];
   112	}
   113	
   114	export interface PipelinesPageData {
   115	  readonly rows: readonly PipelineRow[];
   116	  readonly errors: readonly PipelineErrorRow[];
   117	  /** Total lane count surveyed (active + archived). */
   118	  readonly totalLanes: number;
   119	}
   120	
   121	/**
   122	 * Determine the source of a template id. Override-takes-precedence:
   123	 * an id with both an override and a preset is reported as
   124	 * `project-override` (mirrors the loader's resolution order).
   125	 */
   126	function sourceForId(projectRoot: string, id: string): PipelineSource {
   127	  if (hasPipelineOverride(projectRoot, id)) return 'project-override';
   128	  if (isPluginPresetPipeline(id)) return 'plugin-preset';
   129	  // The enumerator only emits ids whose JSON exists on disk; a
   130	  // disappearing-file race between enumeration and source-classification
   131	  // surfaces as `plugin-preset` so the renderer's load attempt will
   132	  // fail with `missing`, naming the path. This is a non-fallback —
   133	  // we're not pretending the template exists; we're routing the
   134	  // failure to the load-error code path.
   135	  return 'plugin-preset';
   136	}
   137	
   138	/**
   139	 * Resolve the on-disk JSON path for a template id, picking the
   140	 * override path when one exists and falling back to the plugin
   141	 * default. Used for the error-row `path` so the operator can open
   142	 * the offending file.
   143	 */
   144	function pathForId(projectRoot: string, id: string): string {
   145	  if (hasPipelineOverride(projectRoot, id)) {
   146	    return pipelineOverridePath(projectRoot, id);
   147	  }
   148	  return pipelinePluginDefaultPath(id);
   149	}
   150	
   151	/**
   152	 * Classify a thrown loader error into a `PipelineLoadErrorKind` so the
   153	 * renderer can present a tailored hint. The loader's error messages
   154	 * are stable (see `packages/core/src/pipelines/loader.ts`'s
   155	 * `readAndValidate`), so substring matching against those strings is
   156	 * a contract-level signal, not a brittle parse.
   157	 */
   158	function classifyLoadError(message: string): PipelineLoadErrorKind {
   159	  if (message.includes('not found') || message.includes('not valid JSON')) {
   160	    if (message.includes('not valid JSON')) return 'parse';
   161	    return 'missing';
   162	  }
   163	  if (message.includes('failed Zod validation')) return 'zod';
   164	  if (message.includes('declares id') && message.includes('was loaded as')) {
   165	    return 'id-mismatch';
   166	  }
   167	  return 'unknown';
   168	}
   169	
   170	/**
   171	 * Read a lane config's raw JSON for ONLY the `pipelineTemplate`
   172	 * field, without the cross-validating `loadLaneConfig` path that
   173	 * insists the referenced template also resolves. The pipelines page
   174	 * needs to count which lanes reference a given template id even when
   175	 * the template itself is broken — using `loadLaneConfig` would skip
   176	 * those lanes (its loader throws when the cross-validation fails),
   177	 * making a broken template's dependents invisible exactly when the
   178	 * operator most needs to see them.
   179	 *
   180	 * Returns `null` when the file is missing or its JSON cannot be
   181	 * parsed or the `pipelineTemplate` field is not a string. The
   182	 * caller treats those lanes as "no reference here" — the lanes page
   183	 * surfaces the lane-side defect.
   184	 */
   185	function readLanePipelineTemplate(
   186	  projectRoot: string,
   187	  laneId: string,
   188	): string | null {
   189	  const path = join(projectRoot, '.deskwork', 'lanes', `${laneId}.json`);
   190	  if (!existsSync(path)) return null;
   191	  let raw: string;
   192	  try {
   193	    raw = readFileSync(path, 'utf8');
   194	  } catch {
   195	    return null;
   196	  }
   197	  let parsed: unknown;
   198	  try {
   199	    parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
   200	  } catch {
   201	    return null;
   202	  }
   203	  if (
   204	    parsed === null
   205	    || typeof parsed !== 'object'
   206	    || !('pipelineTemplate' in parsed)
   207	  ) {
   208	    return null;
   209	  }
   210	  // After the `in` narrowing, `parsed.pipelineTemplate` is `unknown` —
   211	  // no cast needed; the runtime `typeof` check below is the type
   212	  // guard. Returning `null` for non-string values is the contract
   213	  // (callers treat the lane as "no reference here").
   214	  const value: unknown = parsed.pipelineTemplate;
   215	  return typeof value === 'string' ? value : null;
   216	}
   217	
   218	/**
   219	 * Build an inverse map from templateId → referencing lane ids. Walks
   220	 * every lane config (active + archived) ONCE, reading each lane's raw
   221	 * JSON for its `pipelineTemplate` field (via `readLanePipelineTemplate`
   222	 * — see that function's docstring for why this bypasses
   223	 * `loadLaneConfig`). Lanes whose `pipelineTemplate` cannot be read
   224	 * (missing file, malformed JSON, non-string field) are silently
   225	 * skipped — the lanes page surfaces those defects on its own surface.
   226	 *
   227	 * O(M) disk reads (where M is lane count). Replaces the prior O(N*M)
   228	 * pattern that re-walked every lane for each template.
   229	 */
   230	function buildLaneRefIndex(
   231	  projectRoot: string,
   232	  laneIds: readonly string[],
   233	): Map<string, string[]> {
   234	  const index = new Map<string, string[]>();
   235	  for (const laneId of laneIds) {
   236	    const templateId = readLanePipelineTemplate(projectRoot, laneId);
   237	    if (templateId === null) continue;
   238	    const existing = index.get(templateId);
   239	    if (existing === undefined) {
   240	      index.set(templateId, [laneId]);
   241	    } else {
   242	      existing.push(laneId);
   243	    }
   244	  }
   245	  return index;
   246	}
   247	
   248	/**
   249	 * Build a `PipelineRow` from a successfully-loaded template. The
   250	 * `linearStages` / `lockedStages` / `offPipelineStages` arrays are
   251	 * defensively re-copied as frozen arrays so the renderer can iterate
   252	 * without aliasing the loader's internal state.
   253	 */
   254	function rowFromTemplate(
   255	  id: string,
   256	  source: PipelineSource,
   257	  template: PipelineTemplate,
   258	  referencingLanes: readonly string[],
   259	): PipelineRow {
   260	  return {
   261	    id,
   262	    source,
   263	    name: template.name,
   264	    description: template.description,
   265	    linearStages: [...template.linearStages],
   266	    lockedStages:
   267	      template.lockedStages === undefined ? [] : [...template.lockedStages],
   268	    offPipelineStages: [...template.offPipelineStages],
   269	    referencingLanes,
   270	  };
   271	}
   272	
   273	/**
   274	 * Load the full pipelines-page data view. Resolves every enumerated
   275	 * template id through `loadPipelineTemplate`; healthy loads land in
   276	 * `rows`, failures land in `errors` with the offending path + kind +
   277	 * verbatim message. Lane-reference counts are computed once per
   278	 * template id against the active+archived lane set.
   279	 *
   280	 * @param projectRoot - Absolute project root.
   281	 */
   282	export async function loadPipelinesPageData(
   283	  projectRoot: string,
   284	): Promise<PipelinesPageData> {
   285	  const templateIds = listAvailablePipelineTemplates(projectRoot);
   286	  const laneIds = listLaneConfigs(projectRoot, { includeArchived: true });
   287	
   288	  // Build the lane-references index ONCE before iterating templates so
   289	  // template-row construction is O(1) lookup per template rather than
   290	  // a fresh O(M) walk per template (which was the prior O(N*M) shape).
   291	  const laneRefs = buildLaneRefIndex(projectRoot, laneIds);
   292	
   293	  const rows: PipelineRow[] = [];
   294	  const errors: PipelineErrorRow[] = [];
   295	
   296	  for (const id of templateIds) {
   297	    const source = sourceForId(projectRoot, id);
   298	    const referencingLanes = laneRefs.get(id) ?? [];
   299	    try {
   300	      const template = loadPipelineTemplate(id, projectRoot);
   301	      rows.push(rowFromTemplate(id, source, template, referencingLanes));
   302	    } catch (err) {
   303	      const message = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
   304	      const error: PipelineLoadError = {
   305	        kind: classifyLoadError(message),
   306	        path: pathForId(projectRoot, id),
   307	        message,
   308	      };
   309	      errors.push({ id, source, error, referencingLanes });
   310	    }
   311	  }
   312	
   313	  return {
   314	    rows,
   315	    errors,
   316	    totalLanes: laneIds.length,
   317	  };
   318	}

     1	/**
     2	 * Client controller for the `/dev/lanes` studio page (Phase 6 Task
     3	 * 6.3).
     4	 *
     5	 * Responsibilities:
     6	 *
     7	 *   1. **Live command preview.** Each form (New + per-row Edit)
     8	 *      carries a `<code data-lanes-preview>` element. On every
     9	 *      change event the controller rebuilds the preview to match
    10	 *      the form's current values.

    12	 *   2. **Clipboard copy.** Each copy button (`[data-lanes-copy-button]`
    13	 *      on forms, `[data-lane-copy]` on table rows) clipboards its
    14	 *      payload through `copyOrShowFallback` and flashes a "Copied"
    15	 *      affirmation on the button.

    17	 *   3. **Per-row Edit toggle (single-open accordion).** Each row's
    18	 *      Edit button toggles the sibling `tr[data-lane-edit-row]`
    19	 *      between visible / hidden + flips `aria-expanded` on the
    20	 *      toggle button. Opening one row's edit form auto-closes any
    21	 *      previously-open row — at most one edit form is visible at a
    22	 *      time.
    23	 *
    24	 *   4. **Archived-section open-state persistence.** A `toggle` event
    25	 *      handler on `[data-lanes-archived-details]` writes the open
    26	 *      state to `localStorage` (project-scoped); on init the page
    27	 *      reads it back and restores the previous state.
    28	 *
    29	 *   5. **Empty-state CTA focus.** The "Create your first lane" CTA
    30	 *      overrides its anchor scroll to focus the first field of the
    31	 *      New Lane form — the operator's intent on click is "let me
    32	 *      start typing," not "scroll me there." The anchor `href`
    33	 *      stays as a no-JS fallback.
    34	 *
    35	 * Slash-command quoting convention: every operator-supplied value
    36	 * routed through `quoteValue()` (JSON.stringify). This handles
    37	 * embedded quotes, backslashes, and whitespace symmetrically across
    38	 * every flag — name, template, contentDir, id. Cleared fields in
    39	 * the Edit form are NOT emitted as `--flag ""`; to clear a field's
    40	 * value, manually edit the slash-command after pasting (the Edit
    41	 * form is a copy-builder, not a destructive editor).
    42	 *
    43	 * THESIS Consequence 2: the controller never mutates state on the
    44	 * server. There are no fetch / POST paths; every operator action
    45	 * resolves to a clipboard write + a paste in Claude Code.
    46	 *
    47	 * Idempotent: if the page has no `[data-lanes-container]`, init
    48	 * is a no-op. This lets the same script bundle load on multiple
    49	 * surfaces without per-surface guard checks at the import site.

    52	import { copyAndFlash, quoteValue } from '../copy-builder.ts';
    53	import { resolveProjectKey } from '../dashboard/swimlane-storage.ts';
    54	
    55	const ARCHIVED_OPEN_STORAGE_PREFIX = 'deskwork:lanes:';
    56	const ARCHIVED_OPEN_STORAGE_SUFFIX = ':archived-open';
    57	
    58	interface NewFormValues {
    59	  readonly id: string;
    60	  readonly name: string;
    61	  readonly template: string;
    62	  readonly contentDir: string;
    63	}
    64	
    65	interface EditFormValues {
    66	  readonly name: string;
    67	  readonly nameCurrent: string;
    68	  readonly template: string;
    69	  readonly templateCurrent: string;
    70	  readonly contentDir: string;
    71	  readonly contentDirCurrent: string;
    72	}
    73	
    74	/**
    75	 * Module-level tracker for the currently-open Edit form row. Used to
    76	 * implement the single-open accordion: opening a new row's Edit form
    77	 * automatically closes the previously-open one.
    78	 */
    79	let openLaneId: string | null = null;
    80	
    81	function readFieldValue(form: HTMLElement, name: string): string {
    82	  const el = form.querySelector<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>(
    83	    `[data-lanes-field="${name}"]`,
    84	  );
    85	  return el?.value.trim() ?? '';
    86	}
    87	
    88	function readFieldCurrent(form: HTMLElement, name: string): string {
    89	  const el = form.querySelector<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>(
    90	    `[data-lanes-field="${name}"]`,
    91	  );
    92	  return el?.dataset.current ?? '';
    93	}
    94	
    95	function buildCreateCommand(values: NewFormValues): string {
    96	  const id = values.id.length > 0 ? quoteValue(values.id) : '<id>';
    97	  const template =
    98	    values.template.length > 0 ? quoteValue(values.template) : '<template>';
    99	  const contentDir =
   100	    values.contentDir.length > 0 ? quoteValue(values.contentDir) : '<path>';
   101	  const nameFragment =
   102	    values.name.length > 0 ? ` --name ${quoteValue(values.name)}` : '';
   103	  return `/deskwork:lane create ${id} --template ${template} --content-dir ${contentDir}${nameFragment}`;
   104	}
   105	
   106	/**
   107	 * Build the `/deskwork:lane update` command from edit-form values.
   108	 *
   109	 * Cleared fields are NOT emitted as `--flag ""`. Every diff-emit
   110	 * branch requires the new value to be non-empty AND different from
   111	 * the current value — the Edit form is a copy-builder, not a
   112	 * destructive editor. An operator who wants to clear a value
   113	 * manually edits the resulting slash-command after pasting.
   114	 *
   115	 * Operator-supplied values flow through `quoteValue()` to keep
   116	 * quoting symmetric across name / template / contentDir.
   117	 */
   118	function buildUpdateCommand(
   119	  laneId: string,
   120	  values: EditFormValues,
   121	): string {
   122	  const flags: string[] = [];
   123	  if (values.name !== values.nameCurrent && values.name.length > 0) {
   124	    flags.push(`--name ${quoteValue(values.name)}`);
   125	  }
   126	  if (values.template !== values.templateCurrent && values.template.length > 0) {
   127	    flags.push(`--template ${quoteValue(values.template)}`);
   128	  }
   129	  if (
   130	    values.contentDir !== values.contentDirCurrent &&
   131	    values.contentDir.length > 0
   132	  ) {
   133	    flags.push(`--content-dir ${quoteValue(values.contentDir)}`);
   134	  }
   135	  const flagFragment = flags.length === 0 ? '' : ` ${flags.join(' ')}`;
   136	  return `/deskwork:lane update ${quoteValue(laneId)}${flagFragment}`;
   137	}
   138	
   139	function rebuildNewFormPreview(form: HTMLElement): string {
   140	  const values: NewFormValues = {
   141	    id: readFieldValue(form, 'id'),
   142	    name: readFieldValue(form, 'name'),
   143	    template: readFieldValue(form, 'template'),
   144	    contentDir: readFieldValue(form, 'contentDir'),
   145	  };
   146	  const command = buildCreateCommand(values);
   147	  const preview = form.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-lanes-preview]');
   148	  if (preview) preview.textContent = command;
   149	  return command;
   150	}
   151	
   152	function rebuildEditFormPreview(form: HTMLElement, laneId: string): string {
   153	  const values: EditFormValues = {
   154	    name: readFieldValue(form, 'name'),
   155	    nameCurrent: readFieldCurrent(form, 'name'),
   156	    template: readFieldValue(form, 'template'),
   157	    templateCurrent: readFieldCurrent(form, 'template'),
   158	    contentDir: readFieldValue(form, 'contentDir'),
   159	    contentDirCurrent: readFieldCurrent(form, 'contentDir'),
   160	  };
   161	  const command = buildUpdateCommand(laneId, values);
   162	  const preview = form.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-lanes-preview]');
   163	  if (preview) preview.textContent = command;
   164	  return command;
   165	}
   166	
   167	function initNewForm(container: HTMLElement): void {
   168	  const form = container.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-lanes-new-form]');
   169	  if (!form) return;
   170	  const inputs = Array.from(
   171	    form.querySelectorAll<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>('[data-lanes-field]'),
   172	  );
   173	  const rebuild = (): void => {
   174	    rebuildNewFormPreview(form);
   175	  };
   176	  for (const input of inputs) {
   177	    input.addEventListener('input', rebuild);
   178	    input.addEventListener('change', rebuild);
   179	  }
   180	  rebuild();
   181	
   182	  const copyButton = form.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
   183	    '[data-lanes-copy-button="new"]',
   184	  );
   185	  if (copyButton) {
   186	    copyButton.addEventListener('click', async () => {
   187	      const command = rebuildNewFormPreview(form);
   188	      await copyAndFlash(command, copyButton, 'Copied create command');
   189	    });
   190	  }
   191	}
   192	
   193	function initEditForms(container: HTMLElement): void {
   194	  const editForms = Array.from(
   195	    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('[data-lanes-edit-form]'),
   196	  );
   197	  for (const form of editForms) {
   198	    const laneId = form.dataset.laneId;
   199	    if (!laneId) continue;
   200	    const inputs = Array.from(
   201	      form.querySelectorAll<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>('[data-lanes-field]'),
   202	    );
   203	    const rebuild = (): void => {
   204	      rebuildEditFormPreview(form, laneId);
   205	    };
   206	    for (const input of inputs) {
   207	      input.addEventListener('input', rebuild);
   208	      input.addEventListener('change', rebuild);
   209	    }
   210	    rebuild();
   211	
   212	    const copyButton = form.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
   213	      '[data-lanes-copy-button="edit"]',
   214	    );
   215	    if (copyButton) {
   216	      copyButton.addEventListener('click', async () => {
   217	        const command = rebuildEditFormPreview(form, laneId);
   218	        await copyAndFlash(command, copyButton, 'Copied update command');
   219	      });
   220	    }
   221	  }
   222	}
   223	
   224	/**
   225	 * Close the edit-form row for `laneId` and reset its toggle button's
   226	 * `aria-expanded` to `false`. Used by the single-open accordion logic
   227	 * to close the previously-open row when a different row opens.
   228	 */
   229	function closeEditRow(container: HTMLElement, laneId: string): void {
   230	  const row = container.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
   231	    `[data-lane-edit-row][data-lane-id="${laneId}"]`,
   232	  );
   233	  const toggle = container.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
   234	    `[data-lane-edit-toggle][data-lane-id="${laneId}"]`,
   235	  );
   236	  if (row) row.hidden = true;
   237	  if (toggle) toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
   238	}
   239	
   240	function initEditToggles(container: HTMLElement): void {
   241	  const toggles = Array.from(
   242	    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>('[data-lane-edit-toggle]'),
   243	  );
   244	  for (const toggle of toggles) {
   245	    const laneId = toggle.dataset.laneId;
   246	    if (!laneId) continue;
   247	    toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
   248	      const target = container.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
   249	        `[data-lane-edit-row][data-lane-id="${laneId}"]`,
   250	      );
   251	      if (!target) return;
   252	      const willOpen = target.hidden;
   253	      // Single-open accordion: when opening, close any other row's
   254	      // edit form first. When closing, just drop the tracker.
   255	      if (willOpen && openLaneId !== null && openLaneId !== laneId) {
   256	        closeEditRow(container, openLaneId);
   257	      }
   258	      target.hidden = !willOpen;
   259	      toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(willOpen));
   260	      openLaneId = willOpen ? laneId : null;
   261	    });
   262	  }
   263	
   264	  const cancels = Array.from(
   265	    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>('[data-lane-edit-cancel]'),
   266	  );
   267	  for (const cancel of cancels) {
   268	    const laneId = cancel.dataset.laneId;
   269	    if (!laneId) continue;
   270	    cancel.addEventListener('click', () => {
   271	      closeEditRow(container, laneId);
   272	      if (openLaneId === laneId) openLaneId = null;
   273	    });
   274	  }
   275	}
   276	
   277	function initRowCopyButtons(container: HTMLElement): void {
   278	  const buttons = Array.from(
   279	    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>('[data-lane-copy]'),
   280	  );
   281	  for (const button of buttons) {
   282	    button.addEventListener('click', async () => {
   283	      const command = button.dataset.copy;
   284	      if (!command || command.length === 0) {
   285	        return;
   286	      }
   287	      await copyAndFlash(command, button, `Copied ${command}`);
   288	    });
   289	  }
   290	}
   291	
   292	/**
   293	 * Resolve the localStorage key for the archived-section open state.
   294	 * Namespaces by project key (same convention as the dashboard's
   295	 * swimlane storage) so two operators sharing a machine but working on
   296	 * different projects don't see each other's collapse state.
   297	 */
   298	function archivedOpenKey(container: HTMLElement): string {
   299	  const projectKey = resolveProjectKey(container);
   300	  return `${ARCHIVED_OPEN_STORAGE_PREFIX}${projectKey}${ARCHIVED_OPEN_STORAGE_SUFFIX}`;
   301	}
   302	
   303	function initArchivedSection(container: HTMLElement): void {
   304	  const details = container.querySelector<HTMLDetailsElement>(
   305	    '[data-lanes-archived-details]',
   306	  );
   307	  if (!details) return;
   308	  const key = archivedOpenKey(container);
   309	
   310	  // Restore previous open state on init.
   311	  try {
   312	    const stored = window.localStorage.getItem(key);
   313	    if (stored !== null) {
   314	      details.open = stored === 'true';
   315	    }
   316	  } catch {
   317	    // localStorage unavailable (private mode, quota, etc.) — fall
   318	    // through to the server-rendered default (closed). Persistence
   319	    // is best-effort; the page still works without it.
   320	  }
   321	
   322	  details.addEventListener('toggle', () => {
   323	    try {
   324	      window.localStorage.setItem(key, String(details.open));
   325	    } catch {
   326	      // Same posture as the read path: best-effort. A failed write
   327	      // doesn't prevent the operator from toggling the section.
   328	    }
   329	  });
   330	}
   331	
   332	function initEmptyStateCta(container: HTMLElement): void {
   333	  const cta = container.querySelector<HTMLAnchorElement>(
   334	    '[data-lanes-cta-focus]',
   335	  );
   336	  if (!cta) return;
   337	  cta.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
   338	    const first = container.querySelector<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>(
   339	      '[data-lanes-new-form] [data-lanes-field="id"]',
   340	    );
   341	    if (!first) return;
   342	    event.preventDefault();
   343	    first.focus();
   344	  });
   345	}
   346	
   347	/**
   348	 * Wire every interactive control on the lanes page. Idempotent —
   349	 * a missing `[data-lanes-container]` short-circuits, so importing
   350	 * this from a shared bundle on other surfaces is harmless.
   351	 */
   352	export function initLanesPage(): void {
   353	  // Reset module-level state so repeat init calls (e.g. in tests)
   354	  // don't carry an open-row tracker across mounts.
   355	  openLaneId = null;
   356	  const container = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-lanes-container]');
   357	  if (!container) return;
   358	  initNewForm(container);
   359	  initEditForms(container);
   360	  initEditToggles(container);
   361	  initRowCopyButtons(container);
   362	  initArchivedSection(container);
   363	  initEmptyStateCta(container);
   364	}

     4	 *
     5	 * Each active or archived lane row gets an inline edit form
     6	 * rendered in a hidden sibling `<tr>`. The row's Edit button
     7	 * toggles the form's visibility client-side.
     8	 *
     9	 * The form is a CLIENT-SIDE copy-builder. Per THESIS Consequence 2
    10	 * the studio never mutates state — the form's copy button produces
    11	 * `/deskwork:lane update <id> [--name <label>] [--template <id>]
    12	 * [--content-dir <path>]` with ONLY the fields that differ from
    13	 * the current lane config. The client controller in `lanes-page.ts`
    14	 * compares the form's live values against `data-current-*`
    15	 * attributes on each field and rebuilds the slash command on
    16	 * every change event.

    19	 * form does not present an id field.

     1	/**
     2	 * Per-template Edit form renderer for `/dev/pipelines` (Phase 6 Task
     3	 * 6.4 step 6.4.2 + step 6.4.3 — mutation side).
     4	 *
     5	 * Each healthy template row gets an inline edit panel rendered in a
     6	 * hidden sibling `<tr>`. The panel exposes the FIVE mutually-exclusive
     7	 * `pipeline update` operations as their own `<details>` sub-forms.
     8	 * The CLI accepts only one operation per invocation, so the panel
     9	 * reflects that contract by giving each operation its own preview +
    10	 * Copy button. The operator runs the operations one at a time.
    11	 *
    12	 * Sub-forms (mirroring the CLI flags):
    13	 *
    14	 *   1. Add stage — `--add-stage <name> [--position N]`
    15	 *   2. Rename stage — `--rename-stage <from> --to-stage <to>`
    16	 *   3. Remove stage — `--remove-stage <name>`
    17	 *   4. Set locked — `--set-locked "<s1>,<s2>,..."`
    18	 *   5. Set off-pipeline — `--set-off-pipeline "<s1>,<s2>,..."`
    19	 *
    20	 * The five panels form a single-open accordion: clicking one opens
    21	 * it and closes any previously-open sibling. The accordion is wired
    22	 * client-side; server-side every panel renders closed.
    23	 *
    24	 * Plugin-preset templates get a notice at the top of the panel
    25	 * directing the operator to `/deskwork:customize pipeline <id>`
    26	 * before mutating — the CLI refuses to mutate a plugin preset, and
    27	 * surfacing the refusal here means the operator doesn't have to
    28	 * paste a copy command into Claude Code to learn the gate exists.
    29	 */
    30	
    31	import { html, unsafe, type RawHtml } from '../html.ts';
    32	import type { PipelineRow } from './data.ts';
    33	
    34	function renderCustomizeNotice(row: PipelineRow): RawHtml {
    35	  if (row.source !== 'plugin-preset') return unsafe('');
    36	  return unsafe(html`
    37	    <div class="pipelines-edit-notice" role="status">
    38	      <strong>Plugin preset — customize first.</strong>
    39	      Plugin-shipped templates are read-only. To mutate, run
    40	      <code>/deskwork:customize pipeline ${row.id}</code> first;
    41	      that writes a project-override under <code>.deskwork/pipelines/${row.id}.json</code>
    42	      which the update operations below can then mutate.
    43	    </div>`);
    44	}

    28	 *      as a single-open accordion: opening one closes the others.

    30	 *      one update operation runs per invocation.

    33	 * `quoteValue()` (JSON.stringify). The CLI accepts the resulting
    34	 * double-quoted, backslash-escaped form for every flag.

    38	 * surface; both inits run on every page and short-circuit when their
    39	 * markers are absent.

    41	 * THESIS Consequence 2: the controller never mutates state on the
    42	 * server. There are no fetch / POST paths; every operator action
    43	 * resolves to a clipboard write + paste in Claude Code.

    46	import { copyAndFlash } from '../copy-builder.ts';

    48	  buildCreateCommand,
    49	  buildEditCommand,
    50	  UPDATE_OPS,
    51	  type BuildResult,
    52	  type UpdateOp,
    53	} from './pipelines-builders.ts';
    54	
    55	/**
    56	 * Module-level tracker for the currently-open per-row panel (View or
    57	 * Edit). Each entry is `{ pipelineId, panel: 'view'|'edit' }`. Used
    58	 * by the single-open accordion logic so opening any panel auto-closes
    59	 * the previously-open one (cross-row AND cross-panel).
    60	 */
    61	interface OpenPanelState {
    62	  readonly pipelineId: string;
    63	  readonly panel: 'view' | 'edit';
    64	}
    65	
    66	let openPanel: OpenPanelState | null = null;

    68	function rebuildNewPreview(form: HTMLElement): BuildResult {
    69	  const result = buildCreateCommand(form);
    70	  const preview = form.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
    71	    '[data-pipelines-preview="new"]',
    72	  );
    73	  if (preview) preview.textContent = result.command;
    74	  return result;
    75	}
    76	
    77	function rebuildEditPreview(
    78	  form: HTMLElement,
    79	  op: UpdateOp,
    80	  pipelineId: string,
    81	): BuildResult {
    82	  const result = buildEditCommand(form, op, pipelineId);
    83	  const preview = form.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
    84	    `[data-pipelines-preview="${op}"]`,
    85	  );
    86	  if (preview) preview.textContent = result.command;
    87	  return result;
    88	}
    89	
    90	/**
    91	 * Resolve (or lazily create) the inline notice element adjacent to a
    92	 * Copy button. The notice is a sibling `<p>` injected into the Copy
    93	 * button's containing actions block; it shows the validity error when
    94	 * the build result is invalid and is hidden otherwise. Keeping the
    95	 * controller responsible for the notice element (rather than the
    96	 * server-side renderer) means every Copy button — regardless of which
    97	 * sub-form rendered it — gets the same affordance shape automatically.
    98	 */
    99	function resolveNotice(button: HTMLButtonElement): HTMLElement {
   100	  const existing = button.parentElement?.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
   101	    '[data-pipelines-copy-notice]',
   102	  );
   103	  if (existing) return existing;
   104	  const notice = document.createElement('p');
   105	  notice.dataset.pipelinesCopyNotice = '';
   106	  notice.className = 'pipelines-copy-notice';
   107	  notice.hidden = true;
   108	  // Insert AFTER the button so screen-reader order matches visual order
   109	  // (operator focuses the button, hears "disabled", then reads the notice
   110	  // explaining why). When no parent exists (test fixtures may attach the
   111	  // button directly to a container), fall back to inserting nothing —
   112	  // the disabled state alone still prevents the broken paste.
   113	  button.parentElement?.insertBefore(notice, button.nextSibling);
   114	  return notice;
   115	}
   116	
   117	/**
   118	 * Apply a build result to a Copy button + its adjacent inline notice.
   119	 * Disables the button (with `disabled` AND `aria-disabled="true"`) when
   120	 * the result carries a validity error; surfaces the error text in the
   121	 * notice; otherwise enables the button and hides the notice.
   122	 */
   123	function applyResultToCopy(
   124	  button: HTMLButtonElement,
   125	  result: BuildResult,
   126	): void {
   127	  const notice = resolveNotice(button);
   128	  if (result.error === null) {
   129	    button.disabled = false;
   130	    button.removeAttribute('aria-disabled');
   131	    notice.hidden = true;
   132	    notice.textContent = '';
   133	    return;
   134	  }
   135	  button.disabled = true;
   136	  button.setAttribute('aria-disabled', 'true');
   137	  notice.hidden = false;
   138	  notice.textContent = result.error;
   139	}
   140	
   141	function initNewForm(container: HTMLElement): void {
   142	  const form = container.querySelector<HTMLElement>('[data-pipelines-new-form]');
   143	  if (!form) return;
   144	  const inputs = Array.from(
   145	    form.querySelectorAll<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>(
   146	      '[data-pipelines-field]',
   147	    ),
   148	  );
   149	  const copy = form.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
   150	    '[data-pipelines-copy-button="new"]',
   151	  );
   152	  const rebuild = (): void => {
   153	    const result = rebuildNewPreview(form);
   154	    if (copy) applyResultToCopy(copy, result);
   155	  };
   156	  for (const input of inputs) {
   157	    input.addEventListener('input', rebuild);
   158	    input.addEventListener('change', rebuild);
   159	  }
   160	  rebuild();
   161	
   162	  if (copy) {
   163	    copy.addEventListener('click', async () => {
   164	      const result = rebuildNewPreview(form);
   165	      applyResultToCopy(copy, result);
   166	      // Refuse to clipboard a command whose preview still carries the
   167	      // `<id>` / `<stages>` angle-bracket markers. The disabled
   168	      // attribute prevents native clicks, but defense-in-depth: if a
   169	      // stale dispatch reaches this handler, the error re-check stops
   170	      // the clipboard write.
   171	      if (result.error !== null) return;
   172	      await copyAndFlash(result.command, copy, 'Copied create command');
   173	    });
   174	  }
   175	}
   176	
   177	function initEditOpForm(
   178	  panel: HTMLElement,
   179	  op: UpdateOp,
   180	  pipelineId: string,
   181	  isPluginPreset: boolean,
   182	): void {
   183	  const form = panel.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
   184	    `[data-pipelines-op-form="${op}"]`,
   185	  );
   186	  if (!form) return;
   187	  const inputs = Array.from(
   188	    form.querySelectorAll<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>(
   189	      '[data-pipelines-field]',
   190	    ),
   191	  );
   192	  const copy = form.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
   193	    `[data-pipelines-copy-button="${op}"]`,
   194	  );
   195	  const buildForCopy = (): BuildResult => {
   196	    const raw = rebuildEditPreview(form, op, pipelineId);
   197	    // Plugin presets are read-only at the CLI level; the customize
   198	    // command writes a project override the operator can then mutate.
   199	    // Override the build error so every Copy button on a preset panel
   200	    // surfaces the same next-step guidance regardless of field state.
   201	    if (isPluginPreset) {
   202	      return {
   203	        command: raw.command,
   204	        error:
   205	          `Plugin presets are read-only. Run /deskwork:customize pipeline ${pipelineId} first to write a project override, then the Edit operations apply.`,
   206	      };
   207	    }
   208	    return raw;
   209	  };
   210	  const rebuild = (): void => {
   211	    const result = buildForCopy();
   212	    if (copy) applyResultToCopy(copy, result);
   213	  };
   214	  for (const input of inputs) {
   215	    input.addEventListener('input', rebuild);
   216	    input.addEventListener('change', rebuild);
   217	  }
   218	  rebuild();
   219	
   220	  if (copy) {
   221	    copy.addEventListener('click', async () => {
   222	      const result = buildForCopy();
   223	      applyResultToCopy(copy, result);
   224	      // Defense-in-depth: refuse to clipboard a command the build
   225	      // reported as invalid (empty required field, empty stage list,
   226	      // plugin-preset gate, etc.) even if the disabled attribute was
   227	      // bypassed.
   228	      if (result.error !== null) return;
   229	      await copyAndFlash(result.command, copy, `Copied ${op} command`);
   230	    });
   231	  }
   232	}
   233	
   234	/**
   235	 * Wire the single-open accordion across the five `<details
   236	 * data-pipelines-op>` sub-panels inside one Edit panel. Opening any
   237	 * one closes the others — matches the CLI's mutually-exclusive
   238	 * contract.
   239	 */
   240	function initEditSubAccordion(panel: HTMLElement): void {
   241	  const details = Array.from(
   242	    panel.querySelectorAll<HTMLDetailsElement>('[data-pipelines-op]'),
   243	  );
   244	  for (const target of details) {
   245	    target.addEventListener('toggle', () => {
   246	      if (!target.open) return;
   247	      for (const other of details) {
   248	        if (other !== target && other.open) other.open = false;
   249	      }
   250	    });
   251	  }
   252	}
   253	
   254	function initEditPanels(container: HTMLElement): void {
   255	  const panels = Array.from(
   256	    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>('[data-pipelines-edit-panel]'),
   257	  );
   258	  for (const panel of panels) {
   259	    const pipelineId = panel.dataset.pipelineId;
   260	    if (!pipelineId) continue;
   261	    const isPluginPreset =
   262	      panel.dataset.pipelinesSource === 'plugin-preset';
   263	    for (const op of UPDATE_OPS) {
   264	      initEditOpForm(panel, op, pipelineId, isPluginPreset);
   265	    }
   266	    initEditSubAccordion(panel);
   267	  }
   268	}
   269	
   270	/**
   271	 * Close a hidden panel row (View or Edit) and reset its toggle's
   272	 * aria-expanded. Used by the single-open accordion when a sibling
   273	 * panel opens.
   274	 */
   275	function closePanelRow(
   276	  container: HTMLElement,
   277	  pipelineId: string,
   278	  panel: 'view' | 'edit',
   279	): void {
   280	  const rowSelector =
   281	    panel === 'view' ? 'data-pipeline-view-row' : 'data-pipeline-edit-row';
   282	  const toggleSelector =
   283	    panel === 'view' ? 'data-pipeline-view-toggle' : 'data-pipeline-edit-toggle';
   284	  const row = container.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
   285	    `[${rowSelector}][data-pipeline-id="${pipelineId}"]`,
   286	  );
   287	  const toggle = container.querySelector<HTMLButtonElement>(
   288	    `[${toggleSelector}][data-pipeline-id="${pipelineId}"]`,
   289	  );
   290	  if (row) row.hidden = true;
   291	  if (toggle) toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
   292	}
   293	
   294	function initRowToggles(container: HTMLElement): void {
   295	  const wire = (panel: 'view' | 'edit', toggleAttr: string, rowAttr: string): void => {
   296	    const toggles = Array.from(
   297	      container.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>(`[${toggleAttr}]`),
   298	    );
   299	    for (const toggle of toggles) {
   300	      const pipelineId = toggle.dataset.pipelineId;
   301	      if (!pipelineId) continue;
   302	      toggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
   303	        const target = container.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
   304	          `[${rowAttr}][data-pipeline-id="${pipelineId}"]`,
   305	        );
   306	        if (!target) return;
   307	        const willOpen = target.hidden;
   308	        if (willOpen && openPanel !== null) {
   309	          // Close whichever panel was previously open (could be the
   310	          // same row's sibling panel or a different row's panel).
   311	          closePanelRow(container, openPanel.pipelineId, openPanel.panel);
   312	        }
   313	        target.hidden = !willOpen;
   314	        toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(willOpen));
   315	        openPanel = willOpen ? { pipelineId, panel } : null;
   316	      });
   317	    }
   318	  };
   319	  wire('view', 'data-pipeline-view-toggle', 'data-pipeline-view-row');
   320	  wire('edit', 'data-pipeline-edit-toggle', 'data-pipeline-edit-row');
   321	
   322	  const cancels = Array.from(
   323	    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>('[data-pipeline-edit-cancel]'),
   324	  );
   325	  for (const cancel of cancels) {
   326	    const pipelineId = cancel.dataset.pipelineId;
   327	    if (!pipelineId) continue;
   328	    cancel.addEventListener('click', () => {
   329	      closePanelRow(container, pipelineId, 'edit');
   330	      if (openPanel?.pipelineId === pipelineId && openPanel.panel === 'edit') {
   331	        openPanel = null;
   332	      }
   333	    });
   334	  }
   335	}
   336	
   337	function initRowCopyButtons(container: HTMLElement): void {
   338	  const buttons = Array.from(
   339	    container.querySelectorAll<HTMLButtonElement>('[data-pipeline-copy]'),
   340	  );
   341	  for (const button of buttons) {
   342	    button.addEventListener('click', async () => {
   343	      const command = button.dataset.copy;
   344	      if (!command || command.length === 0) return;
   345	      await copyAndFlash(command, button, `Copied ${command}`);
   346	    });
   347	  }
   348	}
   349	
   350	/**
   351	 * Wire every interactive control on the pipelines page. Idempotent —
   352	 * absent `[data-pipelines-container]` short-circuits, so importing
   353	 * this from a shared bundle on other surfaces is harmless.
   354	 */
   355	export function initPipelinesPage(): void {
   356	  // Reset module-level state so repeat init calls (e.g. across tests)
   357	  // don't carry a stale open-panel tracker.
   358	  openPanel = null;
   359	  const container = document.querySelector<HTMLElement>(
   360	    '[data-pipelines-container]',
   361	  );
   362	  if (!container) return;
   363	  initNewForm(container);
   364	  initEditPanels(container);
   365	  initRowToggles(container);
   366	  initRowCopyButtons(container);
   367	}

     1	/**
     2	 * Shared copy-builder helper for clipboard-action buttons.
     3	 *
     4	 * Extracted from `lanes/lanes-page.ts` and `pipelines/pipelines-page.ts`
     5	 * after Phase 6 Task 6.4 introduced the second consumer. Both
     6	 * copy-builder controllers (and any future studio surface that ships
     7	 * a "build a slash command via fields, copy the result" affordance —
     8	 * Task 6.5's pipeline-migration tray, etc.) need exactly the same
     9	 * post-copy affirmation: green "Copied ✓" flash for
    10	 * `COPIED_FLASH_MS` then revert.
    11	 *
    12	 * `copyAndFlash` calls `copyOrShowFallback` (the shared clipboard
    13	 * helper). On success it flips the button into the affirmation state;
    14	 * on fallback (insecure context, denied permission) the fallback
    15	 * panel handles operator-side affordance, so the button does NOT
    16	 * flash — the fallback panel IS the feedback signal.
    17	 *
    18	 * Leaf module: imports only from `./clipboard.ts`. No DOM-specific
    19	 * styling lives here — the `.is-copied` class lives in
    20	 * `lanes-page.css` and `pipelines-page.css` (and any consumer
    21	 * stylesheet must define it).
    22	 */
    23	
    24	import { copyOrShowFallback } from './clipboard.ts';
    25	
    26	export const COPIED_FLASH_MS = 1500;
    27	
    28	/**
    29	 * Quote an operator-supplied value for inclusion in a slash command.
    30	 *
    31	 * Uses `JSON.stringify` to wrap the value in double quotes and escape
    32	 * embedded quotes, backslashes, and control characters. Applied
    33	 * uniformly to every value routed into a slash-command builder so
    34	 * the output parses identically across shells and Claude Code's slash
    35	 * parser (and so a value with spaces or quotes can't slip through as
    36	 * an injection surface if pasted into a shell).
    37	 *
    38	 * Shared across `lanes-page.ts`, `pipelines-page.ts`, and any future
    39	 * copy-builder surface — keeping one source of truth ensures the
    40	 * quoting contract is identical across surfaces.
    41	 */
    42	export function quoteValue(value: string): string {
    43	  return JSON.stringify(value);
    44	}
    45	
    46	const FALLBACK_MESSAGE =
    47	  'Clipboard unavailable — select and Cmd-C to copy this command, then paste it into Claude Code:';
    48	
    49	export async function copyAndFlash(
    50	  command: string,
    51	  button: HTMLButtonElement,
    52	  successMessage: string,
    53	): Promise<void> {
    54	  const original = button.textContent;
    55	  const ok = await copyOrShowFallback(command, {
    56	    successMessage,
    57	    fallbackMessage: FALLBACK_MESSAGE,
    58	  });
    59	  if (ok) {
    60	    button.classList.add('is-copied');
    61	    button.textContent = 'Copied ✓';
    62	    window.setTimeout(() => {
    63	      button.classList.remove('is-copied');
    64	      if (original !== null) button.textContent = original;
    65	    }, COPIED_FLASH_MS);
    66	  }
    67	}

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	/**
     2	 * "New pipeline template" form renderer for `/dev/pipelines` (Phase 6
     3	 * Task 6.4 step 6.4.1).
     4	 *
     5	 * Client-side copy-builder mirroring the lanes-page New form. Per
     6	 * THESIS Consequence 2 the studio never mutates state — the form's
     7	 * Copy button clipboards the equivalent
     8	 * `/deskwork:pipeline create <id> --shape "Stage1,Stage2,..."
     9	 * [--name <label>] [--description <text>]` slash command.
    10	 *
    11	 * Required fields: id, shape. Name and description are optional and
    12	 * the CLI uses sensible defaults when omitted; the preview leaves
    13	 * them off when empty.
    14	 *
    15	 * The client controller rebuilds the preview on every change event;
    16	 * the operator-supplied values flow through `quoteValue` for symmetric
    17	 * quoting across all four fields.

     1	/**
     2	 * Studio pipeline-editor page — `/dev/pipelines` (Phase 6 Task 6.4).
     3	 *
     4	 * Server-renders the project's pipeline registry: every plugin-preset
