     8	 * "New pipeline template" copy-builder form composes the equivalent
     9	 * `/deskwork:pipeline create` slash command.
    10	 *
    11	 * Per THESIS Consequence 2, this page never mutates state. Every
    12	 * action button — Copy command, View, Edit-op Copy, Delete — is a
    13	 * clipboard-copy of the equivalent `/deskwork:pipeline <verb>` slash
    14	 * command. The studio's job is to route the operator's intent into a
    15	 * paste-ready command with the right arguments pre-filled.
    16	 *
    17	 * Per the Phase 2 follow-up captured in the workplan, the data layer
    18	 * surfaces malformed override JSON as error rows rather than

    26	 *   - Masthead ("Pipelines" title + lane-binding meta + back link)
    27	 *   - Main container
    28	 *     - Header (page heading + count meta + integrity banner)
    29	 *     - New template form
    30	 *     - Pipeline table (healthy rows + error rows)
    31	 *   - Toast slot (success / fallback panel)
    32	 *
    33	 * The page loads the `editorial-studio-client` bundle for the
    34	 * cross-cutting affordances (folio nav state, masthead popover, copy
    35	 * vocabulary) and `pipelines-page.css` for the page-specific chrome.
    36	 * The pipeline-page client controller lives inside the same bundle
    37	 * as `initPipelinesPage`, registered alongside `initLanesPage`.
    38	 */
    39	
    40	import type { StudioContext } from '../routes/api.ts';
    41	import { html, unsafe, type RawHtml } from './html.ts';
    42	import { layout } from './layout.ts';
    43	import { renderEditorialFolio } from './chrome.ts';
    44	import { renderMasthead } from './masthead.ts';
    45	import { renderMastheadMenu } from './masthead-menu.ts';
    46	import {
    47	  loadPipelinesPageData,
    48	  type PipelinesPageData,
    49	} from './pipelines/data.ts';
    50	import { renderPipelineTable } from './pipelines/table.ts';
    51	import { renderNewPipelineForm } from './pipelines/new-form.ts';
    52	import { renderErrorBanner } from './pipelines/error-banner.ts';
    53	
    54	export async function renderPipelinesPage(ctx: StudioContext): Promise<string> {
    55	  const data = await loadPipelinesPageData(ctx.projectRoot);
    56	
    57	  const masthead = renderMasthead({
    58	    kicker: 'Pipeline registry',
    59	    title: 'Pipelines',
    60	    metaInline: pipelinesMastheadMeta(data),
    61	    isHub: false,
    62	  });
    63	
    64	  const header = renderHeader(data);
    65	  const newForm = renderNewPipelineForm();
    66	  const errorBanner = renderErrorBanner(data.errors);
    67	  const table = renderPipelineTable({
    68	    rows: data.rows,
    69	    errors: data.errors,
    70	  });
    71	
    72	  const body = html`
    73	    ${masthead}
    74	    ${renderMastheadMenu()}
    75	    ${renderEditorialFolio('dashboard', 'the pipeline registry')}
    76	    <main class="er-container pipelines-container" data-pipelines-container>
    77	      ${header}
    78	      ${errorBanner}
    79	      ${newForm}
    80	      <section class="pipelines-table-section" aria-labelledby="pipelines-table-heading">
    81	        <h2 class="pipelines-section-heading" id="pipelines-table-heading">Templates</h2>
    82	        ${table}
    83	      </section>
    84	    </main>
    85	    <div class="er-toast" data-toast hidden></div>`;
    86	
    87	  return layout({
    88	    title: 'Pipelines — dev',
    89	    cssHrefs: [
    90	      '/static/css/editorial-review.css',
    91	      '/static/css/editorial-nav.css',
    92	      '/static/css/editorial-studio.css',
    93	      '/static/css/pipelines-page.css',
    94	      '/static/css/pipelines-stage-flow.css',
    95	    ],
    96	    bodyAttrs: 'data-review-ui="pipelines"',
    97	    bodyHtml: body,
    98	    scriptModules: ['editorial-studio-client'],
    99	  });
   100	}
   101	
   102	function pipelinesMastheadMeta(data: PipelinesPageData): string {
   103	  const healthy = data.rows.length;
   104	  const errorFragment =
   105	    data.errors.length > 0 ? ` · ${data.errors.length} error${data.errors.length === 1 ? '' : 's'}` : '';
   106	  const noun = data.totalLanes === 1 ? 'lane' : 'lanes';
   107	  return `${healthy} template${healthy === 1 ? '' : 's'}${errorFragment} · ${data.totalLanes} ${noun}`;
   108	}
   109	
   110	function renderHeader(data: PipelinesPageData): RawHtml {
   111	  const counts =
   112	    data.errors.length === 0
   113	      ? ''
   114	      : unsafe(html`
   115	        <span class="pipelines-header-warn" role="status">
   116	          ${data.errors.length} template${unsafe(data.errors.length === 1 ? '' : 's')} failed to load — fix the offending JSON before running update / delete.
   117	        </span>`);
   118	  return unsafe(html`
   119	    <header class="er-pagehead pipelines-header" data-pipelines-header>
   120	      <p class="er-pagehead__kicker">Pipeline registry</p>
   121	      <h1 class="er-pagehead__title">Pipelines</h1>
   122	      <p class="er-pagehead__deck">
   123	        Pipeline templates name the stages a lane's entries flow through.
   124	        Every action on this page copies the equivalent
   125	        <code>/deskwork:pipeline</code> command to your clipboard —
   126	        paste into Claude Code to run.
   127	      </p>
   128	      ${counts}
   129	    </header>`);
   130	}

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	/**
     2	 * HTML tagged-template helper.
     3	 *
     4	 * `html` escapes interpolated values by default. `unsafe(s)` wraps a
     5	 * pre-built HTML string in an opaque marker so the tag inlines it raw.
     6	 *
     7	 * Behaviour summary for interpolated values:
     8	 *   - `null` / `undefined` / `false`        → ''
     9	 *   - `unsafe(...)` (object with `__raw`)   → inserted verbatim
    10	 *   - Array<string>                          → joined with no separator
    11	 *     (so `${items.map(i => html`...`)}` Just Works)
    12	 *   - everything else                        → escaped via `escapeHtml`
    13	 *
    14	 * No JSX, no virtual DOM — just string concatenation. The studio is a
    15	 * tiny dev-only surface, so the simplest thing that gets escaping
    16	 * right is the right thing.
    17	 */
    18	
    19	/** Marker shape for raw-HTML embeds. */
    20	export interface RawHtml {
    21	  readonly __raw: string;
    22	}
    23	
    24	/** Wrap a pre-built HTML string so the `html` tag inlines it without escaping. */
    25	export function unsafe(s: string): RawHtml {
    26	  return { __raw: s };
    27	}
    28	
    29	/** Type guard for `unsafe(...)` values. */
    30	function isRaw(value: unknown): value is RawHtml {
    31	  return (
    32	    typeof value === 'object' &&
    33	    value !== null &&
    34	    '__raw' in value &&
    35	    typeof (value as { __raw: unknown }).__raw === 'string'
    36	  );
    37	}
    38	
    39	/**
    40	 * Escape a string for safe insertion into HTML text or attribute context.
    41	 * `&` first, then `<`, `>`, `"`, `'`. The single-quote escape lets the
    42	 * same function serve both contexts without a separate `escapeAttr`.
    43	 */
    44	export function escapeHtml(s: string): string {
    45	  return s
    46	    .replaceAll('&', '&amp;')
    47	    .replaceAll('<', '&lt;')
    48	    .replaceAll('>', '&gt;')
    49	    .replaceAll('"', '&quot;')
    50	    .replaceAll("'", '&#39;');
    51	}
    52	
    53	function renderValue(value: unknown): string {
    54	  if (value === null || value === undefined || value === false) return '';
    55	  if (isRaw(value)) return value.__raw;
    56	  if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.map(renderValue).join('');
    57	  if (typeof value === 'string') return escapeHtml(value);
    58	  if (typeof value === 'number' || typeof value === 'bigint') return String(value);
    59	  if (typeof value === 'boolean') return value ? 'true' : '';
    60	  // Stringify objects defensively — the only legitimate object case is the
    61	  // `unsafe(...)` marker, which we handled above. Anything else is a
    62	  // template author bug; show it loudly so it gets caught in tests.
    63	  return escapeHtml(String(value));
    64	}
    65	
    66	/**
    67	 * Tagged-template helper. Static parts go in verbatim; interpolated
    68	 * values run through `renderValue`.
    69	 */
    70	export function html(
    71	  strings: TemplateStringsArray,
    72	  ...values: unknown[]
    73	): string {
    74	  let out = '';
    75	  for (let i = 0; i < strings.length; i++) {
    76	    out += strings[i];
    77	    if (i < values.length) out += renderValue(values[i]);
    78	  }
    79	  return out;
    80	}

    83	export { gloss } from '../lib/glossary-helper.ts';
    84	export type { GlossaryKey } from '../lib/glossary-helper.ts';

     1	/**
     2	 * Pure slash-command builders for `/dev/pipelines` (Phase 6 Task 6.4).
     3	 *
     4	 * Extracted from `pipelines-page.ts` to keep the controller module
     5	 * under the project's 500-line file cap. Each `buildXxxCommand`
     6	 * function reads from a DOM form and returns the assembled slash
     7	 * command + an optional validity error. The controller wires the
     8	 * results to the live preview + the Copy button's enabled state.
     9	 *
    10	 * Why a `BuildResult` instead of just a string:
    11	 *
    12	 *   `command` is always populated so the live preview can render the
    13	 *   placeholder shape ("…<name>") while the operator fills in fields
    14	 *   — useful feedback during typing. `error` is non-null when one or
    15	 *   more required fields are empty (or a set-stage operation has no
    16	 *   selections, which the CLI's `splitStageList` refuses). When set,
    17	 *   the Copy button is disabled and the inline notice surfaces the
    18	 *   message. This pairs preview-shows-shape (helpful) with
    19	 *   copy-emits-broken-command (the hard stop) — the operator sees the
    20	 *   placeholder but can't paste a CLI-error-prone shape into Claude
    21	 *   Code.
    22	 */
    23	
    24	import { quoteValue } from '../copy-builder.ts';
    25	
    26	/**
    27	 * Pipeline id charset — kebab-case starting with `[a-z0-9]`. Mirrors
    28	 * `PIPELINE_ID_REGEX` in `@deskwork/core/pipelines/loader.ts`; keeping
    29	 * this duplicated client-side avoids a workspace dependency. If the
    30	 * core regex ever changes, the test in `pipelines-page-client.test.ts`
    31	 * will surface the drift.
    32	 */
    33	const PIPELINE_ID_REGEX = /^[a-z0-9][a-z0-9-]*$/;
    34	
    35	/**
    36	 * Integer-string check used by `--position` and any other CLI flag
    37	 * that expects a non-negative integer. Allows empty (caller decides).
    38	 */
    39	const NON_NEGATIVE_INTEGER_REGEX = /^\d+$/;
    40	
    41	/**
    42	 * Split a comma-list value into trimmed entries. Returns `{ entries,
    43	 * hasBlank }`; the caller decides whether `hasBlank` is an error
    44	 * (set-locked / set-off-pipeline / create --shape all refuse it
    45	 * symmetrically per the CLI's `splitStageList`).
    46	 */
    47	function splitCsv(value: string): { entries: string[]; hasBlank: boolean } {
    48	  const parts = value.split(',');
    49	  const entries: string[] = [];
    50	  let hasBlank = false;
    51	  for (const part of parts) {
    52	    const trimmed = part.trim();
    53	    if (trimmed.length === 0) {
    54	      hasBlank = true;
    55	    } else {
    56	      entries.push(trimmed);
    57	    }
    58	  }
    59	  return { entries, hasBlank };
    60	}
    61	
    62	/**
    63	 * The set of operations the Edit panel exposes — one per CLI flag on
    64	 * `deskwork pipeline update`. The CLI rejects multiple operations per
    65	 * invocation; the controller's single-open accordion matches that
    66	 * contract on the UI side.
    67	 */
    68	export type UpdateOp =
    69	  | 'add'
    70	  | 'rename'
    71	  | 'remove'
    72	  | 'set-locked'
    73	  | 'set-off-pipeline';
    74	
    75	export const UPDATE_OPS: readonly UpdateOp[] = [
    76	  'add',
    77	  'rename',
    78	  'remove',
    79	  'set-locked',
    80	  'set-off-pipeline',
    81	];
    82	
    83	export interface BuildResult {
    84	  readonly command: string;
    85	  readonly error: string | null;
    86	}
    87	
    88	/**
    89	 * Read a field's trimmed value from a form. Returns empty string when
    90	 * the field is absent so callers can treat "missing" and "blank" as
    91	 * equivalent for the preview-rebuild path.
    92	 */
    93	function readField(form: HTMLElement, name: string): string {
    94	  const el = form.querySelector<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement>(
    95	    `[data-pipelines-field="${name}"]`,
    96	  );
    97	  return el?.value.trim() ?? '';
    98	}
    99	
   100	/**
   101	 * Read a set of checkbox values (used by the set-locked sub-operation).
   102	 * Returns the values of every checked input in document order.
   103	 */
   104	function readCheckedValues(form: HTMLElement, name: string): string[] {
   105	  const els = Array.from(
   106	    form.querySelectorAll<HTMLInputElement>(
   107	      `input[type="checkbox"][data-pipelines-field="${name}"]`,
   108	    ),
   109	  );
   110	  return els.filter((el) => el.checked).map((el) => el.value);
   111	}
   112	
   113	function missingFieldsError(missing: readonly string[]): string | null {
   114	  if (missing.length === 0) return null;
   115	  const noun = missing.length === 1 ? 'field' : 'fields';
   116	  return `Fill required ${noun}: ${missing.join(', ')}.`;
   117	}
   118	
   119	/** Build the `/deskwork:pipeline create` command from the New form. */
   120	export function buildCreateCommand(form: HTMLElement): BuildResult {
   121	  const id = readField(form, 'new-id');
   122	  const shape = readField(form, 'new-shape');
   123	  const name = readField(form, 'new-name');
   124	  const description = readField(form, 'new-description');
   125	
   126	  const idArg = id.length > 0 ? quoteValue(id) : '<id>';
   127	  const shapeArg = shape.length > 0 ? quoteValue(shape) : '<stages>';
   128	  const nameFragment = name.length > 0 ? ` --name ${quoteValue(name)}` : '';
   129	  const descFragment =
   130	    description.length > 0 ? ` --description ${quoteValue(description)}` : '';
   131	  const command = `/deskwork:pipeline create ${idArg} --shape ${shapeArg}${nameFragment}${descFragment}`;
   132	
   133	  const missing: string[] = [];
   134	  if (id.length === 0) missing.push('id');
   135	  if (shape.length === 0) missing.push('shape');
   136	  const missingError = missingFieldsError(missing);
   137	  if (missingError !== null) return { command, error: missingError };
   138	
   139	  if (!PIPELINE_ID_REGEX.test(id)) {
   140	    return {
   141	      command,
   142	      error:
   143	        `Invalid pipeline id "${id}". Use kebab-case [a-z0-9-] starting with [a-z0-9].`,
   144	    };
   145	  }
   146	  const { hasBlank } = splitCsv(shape);
   147	  if (hasBlank) {
   148	    return {
   149	      command,
   150	      error: 'Shape contains a blank stage (consecutive commas). Remove the empty entry.',
   151	    };
   152	  }
   153	  return { command, error: null };
   154	}
   155	
   156	/** Build the `/deskwork:pipeline update <id> --add-stage ...` command. */
   157	export function buildAddCommand(form: HTMLElement, pipelineId: string): BuildResult {
   158	  const name = readField(form, 'add-name');
   159	  const position = readField(form, 'add-position');
   160	  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
   161	  const nameArg = name.length > 0 ? quoteValue(name) : '<name>';
   162	  const positionFragment =
   163	    position.length > 0 ? ` --position ${position}` : '';
   164	  const command = `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --add-stage ${nameArg}${positionFragment}`;
   165	  if (name.length === 0) {
   166	    return { command, error: 'Fill required field: stage name.' };
   167	  }
   168	  if (position.length > 0 && !NON_NEGATIVE_INTEGER_REGEX.test(position)) {
   169	    return {
   170	      command,
   171	      error: `Invalid position "${position}". Use a non-negative integer (0-indexed).`,
   172	    };
   173	  }
   174	  return { command, error: null };
   175	}
   176	
   177	/** Build the `--rename-stage <from> --to-stage <to>` command. */
   178	export function buildRenameCommand(
   179	  form: HTMLElement,
   180	  pipelineId: string,
   181	): BuildResult {
   182	  const from = readField(form, 'rename-from');
   183	  const to = readField(form, 'rename-to');
   184	  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
   185	  const fromArg = from.length > 0 ? quoteValue(from) : '<from>';
   186	  const toArg = to.length > 0 ? quoteValue(to) : '<to>';
   187	  const command = `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --rename-stage ${fromArg} --to-stage ${toArg}`;
   188	
   189	  const missing: string[] = [];
   190	  if (from.length === 0) missing.push('from');
   191	  if (to.length === 0) missing.push('to');
   192	  return { command, error: missingFieldsError(missing) };
   193	}
   194	
   195	/** Build the `--remove-stage <name>` command. */
   196	export function buildRemoveCommand(
   197	  form: HTMLElement,
   198	  pipelineId: string,
   199	): BuildResult {
   200	  const name = readField(form, 'remove-name');
   201	  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
   202	  const nameArg = name.length > 0 ? quoteValue(name) : '<name>';
   203	  const command = `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --remove-stage ${nameArg}`;
   204	  const error = name.length === 0 ? 'Pick a stage to remove.' : null;
   205	  return { command, error };
   206	}
   207	
   208	/** Build the `--set-locked "s1,s2,..."` command. */
   209	export function buildSetLockedCommand(
   210	  form: HTMLElement,
   211	  pipelineId: string,
   212	): BuildResult {
   213	  const checked = readCheckedValues(form, 'set-locked');
   214	  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
   215	  const csv = checked.join(',');
   216	  const command = `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --set-locked ${quoteValue(csv)}`;
   217	  // The CLI's `splitStageList` rejects an empty comma-separated list
   218	  // (exit 2). Surface the gate here so the operator who unchecks every
   219	  // box doesn't stumble into a broken paste. The lock set lives on the
   220	  // pipeline template (not lanes); there's no CLI verb today to "clear
   221	  // all locks," so the escape hatch is direct file edit. Renaming or
   222	  // removing a stage through the Add/Rename/Remove panels above also
   223	  // drops its locked-state as a side effect.
   224	  const error =
   225	    checked.length === 0
   226	      ? 'Cannot clear all locked stages via --set-locked (the CLI rejects an empty list). '
   227	        + 'There is no CLI verb to clear locks today — edit '
   228	        + '.deskwork/pipelines/<id>.json directly to remove entries from lockedStages. '
   229	        + '(Renaming or removing a stage above also drops its locked-state as a side effect.)'
   230	      : null;
   231	  return { command, error };
   232	}
   233	
   234	/** Build the `--set-off-pipeline "s1,s2,..."` command. */
   235	export function buildSetOffCommand(
   236	  form: HTMLElement,
   237	  pipelineId: string,
   238	): BuildResult {
   239	  const csv = readField(form, 'set-off-pipeline');
   240	  const idArg = quoteValue(pipelineId);
   241	  const command = `/deskwork:pipeline update ${idArg} --set-off-pipeline ${quoteValue(csv)}`;
   242	  // Same CLI gate as set-locked: an empty value reaches `splitStageList`
   243	  // which rejects it (exit 2). Surface the gate symmetrically.
   244	  if (csv.length === 0) {
   245	    return {
   246	      command,
   247	      error:
   248	        'Cannot clear all off-pipeline stages via --set-off-pipeline (the CLI '
   249	        + 'rejects an empty list). To remove individual stages, edit '
   250	        + '.deskwork/pipelines/<id>.json directly.',
   251	    };
   252	  }
   253	  const { hasBlank } = splitCsv(csv);
   254	  if (hasBlank) {
   255	    return {
   256	      command,
   257	      error: 'Off-pipeline list contains a blank entry (consecutive commas). Remove the empty entry.',
   258	    };
   259	  }
   260	  return { command, error: null };

     1	/**
     2	 * deskwork-pipeline — CRUD operations on pipeline templates.
     3	 *
     4	 * Phase 6 Task 6.2 (graphical-entries). Thin dispatcher over
     5	 * `@deskwork/core/pipelines` operations:
     6	 *
     7	 *   deskwork pipeline list [--full]                       — enumerate templates
     8	 *   deskwork pipeline show <id>                           — show a single template (resolved JSON)
     9	 *   deskwork pipeline create <id> --shape "<s1>,<s2>,..." [--name <label>] [--description <text>]
    10	 *   deskwork pipeline update <id> --add-stage <name> [--position N]
    11	 *   deskwork pipeline update <id> --rename-stage <from> --to-stage <to>
    12	 *   deskwork pipeline update <id> --remove-stage <name>
    13	 *   deskwork pipeline update <id> --set-locked "<s1>,<s2>,..."
    14	 *   deskwork pipeline update <id> --set-off-pipeline "<s1>,<s2>,..."
    15	 *   deskwork pipeline delete <id> [--reassign-lanes-to <other-id>]
    16	 *
    17	 * Each handler maps the parsed argv onto the matching core operation
    18	 * and emits a structured JSON result on stdout. Errors are routed
    19	 * through `fail` (stderr + non-zero exit).
    20	 *
    21	 * `update`'s five operation flags are mutually exclusive — the
    22	 * handler refuses (exit 2) when more than one is passed in a single
    23	 * invocation. The CLI uses `--to-stage <to>` rather than the workplan
    24	 * shape `--rename-stage <from> <to>` because the underlying argv
    25	 * parser is single-value-per-flag; reading the second positional after
    26	 * `--rename-stage` as `<to>` would require a special-cased parser.
    27	 * `--to-stage` keeps the parser shape uniform and is documented in the
    28	 * SKILL.md.
    29	 */

    80	function genericUsage(): never {
    81	  fail(
    82	    'Usage: deskwork pipeline <project-root> <verb> [args...]\n'
    83	      + '  verbs: list | show | create | update | delete\n'
    84	      + '  see `deskwork pipeline <project-root> <verb>` for per-verb help',
    85	    2,
    86	  );
    87	}
    88	
    89	function verbUsage(verb: string): never {
    90	  const u = VERB_USAGE[verb];
    91	  if (u === undefined) genericUsage();
    92	  fail(`Usage: ${u}`, 2);
    93	}
    94	
    95	export async function run(argv: string[]): Promise<void> {
    96	  let parsed: ParsedArgs;
    97	  try {
    98	    parsed = parseArgs(argv, KNOWN_FLAGS, BOOLEAN_FLAGS);
    99	  } catch (err) {
   100	    fail(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err), 2);
   101	  }
   102	
   103	  const { positional, flags, booleans } = parsed;
   104	  if (positional.length < 2) genericUsage();
   105	
   106	  const [rootArg, verb, ...rest] = positional;
   107	  const projectRoot = absolutize(rootArg);
   108	
   109	  switch (verb) {
   110	    case 'list':
   111	      await handleList(projectRoot, booleans.has('full'));
   112	      return;
   113	    case 'show':
   114	      await handleShow(projectRoot, rest);
   115	      return;
   116	    case 'create':
   117	      await handleCreate(projectRoot, rest, flags);
   118	      return;
   119	    case 'update':
   120	      await handleUpdate(projectRoot, rest, flags);
   121	      return;
   122	    case 'delete':
   123	      await handleDelete(projectRoot, rest, flags);
   124	      return;
   125	    default:
   126	      fail(
   127	        `Unknown pipeline verb: ${verb}\n`
   128	          + '  verbs: list | show | create | update | delete',
   129	        2,
   130	      );
   131	  }
   132	}
   133	
   134	async function handleList(projectRoot: string, full: boolean): Promise<void> {
   135	  try {
   136	    const pipelines = listPipelines(projectRoot);
   137	    if (!full) {
   138	      emit({ pipelines: pipelines.map((p) => ({ id: p.id })) });
   139	      return;
   140	    }
   141	    emit({
   142	      pipelines: pipelines.map((p) => ({
   143	        id: p.id,
   144	        name: p.template.name,
   145	        source: p.source,
   146	        linearStageCount: p.linearStageCount,
   147	        lockedStageCount: p.lockedStageCount,
   148	        offPipelineStageCount: p.offPipelineStageCount,
   149	      })),
   150	    });
   151	  } catch (err) {
   152	    fail(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   153	  }
   154	}
   155	
   156	async function handleShow(projectRoot: string, rest: string[]): Promise<void> {
   157	  if (rest.length < 1) verbUsage('show');

   159	  try {
   160	    const result = showPipeline(projectRoot, id);
   161	    emit({

   163	      name: result.template.name,
   164	      description: result.template.description,

   166	      ...(result.template.lockedStages !== undefined && {
   167	        lockedStages: result.template.lockedStages,
   168	      }),
   169	      offPipelineStages: result.template.offPipelineStages,
   170	      source: result.source,
   171	    });
   172	  } catch (err) {
   173	    fail(err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err));
   174	  }
   175	}

   177	/**
   178	 * Split a comma-separated stage list. Trims whitespace around each
   179	 * entry; refuses empty results.

   181	function splitStageList(raw: string, flagName: string): string[] {
   182	  const parts = raw.split(',').map((s) => s.trim());
   183	  if (parts.length === 0 || (parts.length === 1 && parts[0].length === 0)) {
   184	    fail(`Flag --${flagName} requires a non-empty comma-separated stage list`, 2);
   185	  }
   186	  return parts;
   187	}

   224	/**
   225	 * Build the discriminated `UpdatePipelineOperation` from the parsed
   226	 * flags. Refuses (exit 2) if zero or more-than-one operation flag is
   227	 * present.
   228	 */
   229	function resolveUpdateOperation(
   230	  id: string,
   231	  flags: Record<string, string>,
   232	): UpdatePipelineOperation {
   233	  const present: string[] = [];
   234	  if (flags['add-stage'] !== undefined) present.push('add-stage');
   235	  if (flags['rename-stage'] !== undefined) present.push('rename-stage');
   236	  if (flags['remove-stage'] !== undefined) present.push('remove-stage');
   237	  if (flags['set-locked'] !== undefined) present.push('set-locked');
   238	  if (flags['set-off-pipeline'] !== undefined) present.push('set-off-pipeline');
   239	
   240	  if (present.length === 0) {
   241	    fail(
   242	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": no operation flag supplied. Pass `
   243	      + 'exactly one of --add-stage, --rename-stage, --remove-stage, '
   244	      + '--set-locked, --set-off-pipeline.',
   245	      2,
   246	    );
   247	  }
   248	  if (present.length > 1) {
   249	    fail(
   250	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": operation flags are mutually `
   251	      + `exclusive; received ${present.join(', ')}. Pass exactly one per `
   252	      + `invocation.`,
   253	      2,
   254	    );
   255	  }
   256	
   257	  if (flags['add-stage'] !== undefined) {
   258	    const positionStr = flags['position'];
   259	    let position: number | undefined;
   260	    if (positionStr !== undefined) {

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	/**
     2	 * pipeline update — mutate a project-override pipeline template.
     3	 *
     4	 * Phase 6 Task 6.2 (graphical-entries). Five mutually-exclusive
     5	 * operations the CLI surfaces as flags. Exactly one operation runs per
     6	 * `update` invocation; the CLI handler is responsible for refusing
     7	 * multiply-flagged invocations.
     8	 *
     9	 *   - `add-stage`        — insert `<stage>` into linearStages at
    10	 *                          `<position>` (default = end).
    11	 *   - `rename-stage`     — rename `<from>` to `<to>` wherever it
    12	 *                          appears (linearStages / lockedStages /
    13	 *                          offPipelineStages). Appends a sidecar
    14	 *                          migration entry to
    15	 *                          `migrations/<id>.json` consumed by the
    16	 *                          doctor verb (Phase 6 Task 6.5) for
    17	 *                          affected-entry remediation.
    18	 *   - `remove-stage`     — remove `<stage>` from whichever list
    19	 *                          contains it. Refused when any entry's
    20	 *                          `currentStage` references it.
    21	 *   - `set-locked`       — replace `lockedStages` wholesale.
    22	 *                          Cross-validates the new set is a subset of
    23	 *                          `linearStages`.
    24	 *   - `set-off-pipeline` — replace `offPipelineStages` wholesale.
    25	 *                          Cross-validates disjointness from
    26	 *                          `linearStages`.
    27	 *
    28	 * Refusal modes (shared):
    29	 *   - The id resolves to a plugin preset (read-only). The operator
    30	 *     should run `customize pipeline <preset-id>` to create an
    31	 *     override first.
    32	 *   - No project override exists for `<id>` — `update` requires the
    33	 *     override to be on disk.
    34	 *
    35	 * Emits a `pipeline-update` journal event on success carrying the
    36	 * operation discriminator + before/after fields where appropriate.
    37	 *
    38	 * Layout note (Phase 6 Task 6.2 review fix #1): the rename-migration
    39	 * sidecar lives at `<projectRoot>/.deskwork/pipelines/migrations/<id>.json`,
    40	 * a SIBLING directory of the per-template overrides. Co-locating it
    41	 * with the templates (the original Task 6.2 shape, `<id>-renames.json`
    42	 * in the override dir) caused `pipeline list`'s JSON enumerator to try
    43	 * loading the migration file as a pipeline template; Zod parse failed
    44	 * and the list verb broke after any rename. The migrations subdirectory
    45	 * is invisible to the override enumerator because it's a directory, not
    46	 * a `*.json` file.
    47	 *
    48	 * Concurrency note: this module assumes a single operator at-rest;
    49	 * concurrent `--rename-stage` operations against the same id race on
    50	 * the migrations sidecar and the second writer wins. The PRD documents
    51	 * deskwork as operator-driven; no file-locking is added without
    52	 * explicit operator approval. (Reviewer finding #5, decline-with-
    53	 * reasoning.)
    54	 *
    55	 * Atomicity note: the journal-event append at the bottom of
    56	 * `updatePipeline` is not atomic with the commit + migration write —
    57	 * matches the precedent in lanes operations (Phase 6 Task 6.1) where
    58	 * the same pattern was accepted. (Reviewer finding #11, decline-with-
    59	 * reasoning.)
    60	 */
    61	
    62	import { appendJournalEvent } from '../../journal/append.ts';
    63	import { readAllSidecars } from '../../sidecar/read-all.ts';
    64	import {
    65	  hasPipelineOverride,
    66	  isPluginPresetPipeline,
    67	  loadPipelineTemplate,
    68	  assertSafePipelineId,
    69	} from '../loader.ts';
    70	import { type PipelineTemplate } from '../types.ts';
    71	import { commitPipelineTemplate } from './commit.ts';
    72	import { appendRenameMigration } from './rename-migration.ts';
    73	
    74	export type UpdatePipelineOperation =
    75	  | { readonly op: 'add-stage'; readonly stage: string; readonly position?: number }
    76	  | { readonly op: 'rename-stage'; readonly from: string; readonly to: string }
    77	  | { readonly op: 'remove-stage'; readonly stage: string }
    78	  | { readonly op: 'set-locked'; readonly stages: readonly string[] }
    79	  | { readonly op: 'set-off-pipeline'; readonly stages: readonly string[] };
    80	
    81	export interface UpdatePipelineOptions {
    82	  readonly id: string;
    83	  readonly operation: UpdatePipelineOperation;
    84	}
    85	
    86	export interface UpdatePipelineResult {
    87	  readonly template: PipelineTemplate;
    88	  readonly path: string;
    89	}
    90	
    91	export async function updatePipeline(
    92	  projectRoot: string,
    93	  opts: UpdatePipelineOptions,
    94	): Promise<UpdatePipelineResult> {
    95	  // Reviewer-fix #10: validate the id BEFORE the preset / override
    96	  // checks so a traversed id surfaces as "Invalid pipeline id" rather
    97	  // than leaking the traversed path through the override-missing
    98	  // diagnostic. Idempotent against the subsequent loader-internal
    99	  // call from loadPipelineTemplate.
   100	  assertSafePipelineId(projectRoot, opts.id);
   101	
   102	  // Pre-flight: refuse on read-only presets so the operator gets a
   103	  // pointer to `customize pipeline <id>` rather than a confusing
   104	  // "no override exists" error. The plugin-preset check fires before
   105	  // the override-presence check because a project that hasn't yet
   106	  // customized a preset will fail both — naming the preset surface is
   107	  // the more actionable diagnostic.
   108	  if (
   109	    isPluginPresetPipeline(opts.id)
   110	    && !hasPipelineOverride(projectRoot, opts.id)
   111	  ) {
   112	    throw new Error(
   113	      `Cannot update pipeline "${opts.id}": "${opts.id}" is a built-in `
   114	      + `plugin preset and is read-only. Run `
   115	      + `"deskwork customize pipeline ${opts.id}" to create a project `
   116	      + `override first.`,
   117	    );
   118	  }
   119	
   120	  if (!hasPipelineOverride(projectRoot, opts.id)) {
   121	    throw new Error(
   122	      `Cannot update pipeline "${opts.id}": no project override exists. `
   123	      + `Create one with "deskwork pipeline create ${opts.id} --shape ..." `
   124	      + `or "deskwork customize pipeline ${opts.id}" (to clone a preset).`,
   125	    );
   126	  }
   127	
   128	  const existing = loadPipelineTemplate(opts.id, projectRoot);
   129	  const candidate = applyOperation(existing, opts.operation, opts.id);
   130	
   131	  // Operations that read entry state for refusal-checks run after we
   132	  // have the candidate (so the error includes what's about to change)
   133	  // but before the commit. `remove-stage` is the only such case today.
   134	  if (opts.operation.op === 'remove-stage') {
   135	    await refuseRemoveStageWhenReferenced(
   136	      projectRoot,
   137	      opts.id,
   138	      opts.operation.stage,
   139	    );
   140	  }
   141	
   142	  const { template, path } = commitPipelineTemplate(
   143	    projectRoot,
   144	    opts.id,
   145	    candidate,
   146	    'update',
   147	  );
   148	
   149	  // The rename-stage migration sidecar fires AFTER the commit succeeds
   150	  // so a doomed write doesn't leave a stranded migration entry.
   151	  if (opts.operation.op === 'rename-stage') {
   152	    appendRenameMigration(
   153	      projectRoot,
   154	      opts.id,
   155	      opts.operation.from,
   156	      opts.operation.to,
   157	    );
   158	  }
   159	
   160	  await appendJournalEvent(projectRoot, {
   161	    kind: 'pipeline-update',
   162	    at: new Date().toISOString(),
   163	    pipelineId: opts.id,
   164	    details: buildEventDetails(opts.operation, existing),
   165	  });
   166	
   167	  return { template, path };
   168	}
   169	
   170	/**
   171	 * Apply a single operation to the template, returning a fresh
   172	 * candidate template. Pure function — no I/O.
   173	 */
   174	function applyOperation(
   175	  existing: PipelineTemplate,
   176	  op: UpdatePipelineOperation,
   177	  id: string,
   178	): PipelineTemplate {
   179	  switch (op.op) {
   180	    case 'add-stage':
   181	      return applyAddStage(existing, op.stage, op.position, id);
   182	    case 'rename-stage':
   183	      return applyRenameStage(existing, op.from, op.to, id);
   184	    case 'remove-stage':
   185	      return applyRemoveStage(existing, op.stage, id);
   186	    case 'set-locked':
   187	      return applySetLocked(existing, op.stages, id);
   188	    case 'set-off-pipeline':
   189	      return applySetOffPipeline(existing, op.stages, id);
   190	  }
   191	}
   192	
   193	function applyAddStage(
   194	  existing: PipelineTemplate,
   195	  stage: string,
   196	  position: number | undefined,
   197	  id: string,
   198	): PipelineTemplate {
   199	  if (stage.trim().length === 0) {
   200	    throw new Error(
   201	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": --add-stage value is blank.`,
   202	    );
   203	  }
   204	  const allKnown = collectKnownStages(existing);
   205	  if (allKnown.has(stage)) {
   206	    throw new Error(
   207	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": stage "${stage}" already exists `
   208	      + `in this template.`,
   209	    );
   210	  }
   211	  const linearStages = [...existing.linearStages];
   212	  const insertAt = position ?? linearStages.length;
   213	  if (insertAt < 0 || insertAt > linearStages.length) {
   214	    throw new Error(
   215	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": --position ${insertAt} is out of `
   216	      + `range. linearStages currently has ${linearStages.length} entries; `
   217	      + `pass a value in [0, ${linearStages.length}].`,
   218	    );
   219	  }
   220	  linearStages.splice(insertAt, 0, stage);
   221	  return { ...existing, linearStages };
   222	}
   223	
   224	function applyRenameStage(
   225	  existing: PipelineTemplate,
   226	  from: string,
   227	  to: string,
   228	  id: string,
   229	): PipelineTemplate {
   230	  if (from.trim().length === 0 || to.trim().length === 0) {
   231	    throw new Error(
   232	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": --rename-stage requires both `
   233	      + `<from> and <to> non-empty.`,
   234	    );
   235	  }
   236	  if (from === to) {
   237	    throw new Error(
   238	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": --rename-stage <from> and <to> `
   239	      + `are identical (${from}).`,
   240	    );
   241	  }
   242	  const allKnown = collectKnownStages(existing);
   243	  if (!allKnown.has(from)) {
   244	    throw new Error(
   245	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": stage "${from}" not found. `
   246	      + `Known stages: ${[...allKnown].join(', ')}.`,
   247	    );
   248	  }
   249	  if (allKnown.has(to)) {
   250	    throw new Error(
   251	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": cannot rename to "${to}" — that `
   252	      + `name already exists in this template.`,
   253	    );
   254	  }
   255	  return {
   256	    ...existing,
   257	    linearStages: existing.linearStages.map((s) => (s === from ? to : s)),
   258	    ...(existing.lockedStages !== undefined && {
   259	      lockedStages: existing.lockedStages.map((s) => (s === from ? to : s)),
   260	    }),
   261	    offPipelineStages: existing.offPipelineStages.map((s) =>
   262	      s === from ? to : s,
   263	    ),
   264	  };
   265	}
   266	
   267	function applyRemoveStage(
   268	  existing: PipelineTemplate,
   269	  stage: string,
   270	  id: string,
   271	): PipelineTemplate {
   272	  if (stage.trim().length === 0) {
   273	    throw new Error(
   274	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": --remove-stage value is blank.`,
   275	    );
   276	  }
   277	  const allKnown = collectKnownStages(existing);
   278	  if (!allKnown.has(stage)) {
   279	    throw new Error(
   280	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": stage "${stage}" not found. `
   281	      + `Known stages: ${[...allKnown].join(', ')}.`,
   282	    );
   283	  }
   284	  const linearStages = existing.linearStages.filter((s) => s !== stage);
   285	  if (linearStages.length === 0 && existing.linearStages.length > 0) {
   286	    throw new Error(
   287	      `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": removing "${stage}" would leave `
   288	      + `linearStages empty. A pipeline must have at least one linear stage.`,
   289	    );
   290	  }
   291	  return {
   292	    ...existing,
   293	    linearStages,
   294	    ...(existing.lockedStages !== undefined && {
   295	      lockedStages: existing.lockedStages.filter((s) => s !== stage),
   296	    }),
   297	    offPipelineStages: existing.offPipelineStages.filter((s) => s !== stage),
   298	  };
   299	}
   300	
   301	function applySetLocked(
   302	  existing: PipelineTemplate,
   303	  stages: readonly string[],
   304	  id: string,
   305	): PipelineTemplate {
   306	  const linearSet = new Set(existing.linearStages);
   307	  for (const stage of stages) {
   308	    if (stage.trim().length === 0) {
   309	      throw new Error(
   310	        `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": --set-locked contains a blank entry.`,
   311	      );
   312	    }
   313	    if (!linearSet.has(stage)) {
   314	      throw new Error(
   315	        `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": locked stage "${stage}" is not in `
   316	        + `linearStages (${existing.linearStages.join(', ')}). lockedStages `
   317	        + `must be a subset of linearStages.`,
   318	      );
   319	    }
   320	  }
   321	  return { ...existing, lockedStages: [...stages] };
   322	}
   323	
   324	function applySetOffPipeline(
   325	  existing: PipelineTemplate,
   326	  stages: readonly string[],
   327	  id: string,
   328	): PipelineTemplate {
   329	  const linearSet = new Set(existing.linearStages);
   330	  for (const stage of stages) {
   331	    if (stage.trim().length === 0) {
   332	      throw new Error(
   333	        `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": --set-off-pipeline contains a `
   334	        + `blank entry.`,
   335	      );
   336	    }
   337	    if (linearSet.has(stage)) {
   338	      throw new Error(
   339	        `Cannot update pipeline "${id}": "${stage}" is already in `
   340	        + `linearStages — a stage is either linear OR off-pipeline, not both.`,
   341	      );
   342	    }
   343	  }
   344	  return { ...existing, offPipelineStages: [...stages] };
   345	}
   346	
   347	/**
   348	 * Collect every stage name visible on the template across all three
   349	 * lists. Used for "does this name already exist" refusal checks.
   350	 */
   351	function collectKnownStages(template: PipelineTemplate): Set<string> {
   352	  const set = new Set<string>(template.linearStages);
   353	  if (template.lockedStages !== undefined) {
   354	    for (const s of template.lockedStages) set.add(s);
   355	  }
   356	  for (const s of template.offPipelineStages) set.add(s);
   357	  return set;
   358	}
   359	
   360	/**
   361	 * Refuse `remove-stage` when any entry's `currentStage` still
   362	 * references the doomed stage AND that entry is bound to a lane whose
   363	 * pipelineTemplate is the one being mutated. Walking only the
   364	 * matching-template entries keeps the error message focused — entries
   365	 * in other lanes are unaffected by the mutation.
   366	 */
   367	async function refuseRemoveStageWhenReferenced(
   368	  projectRoot: string,
   369	  pipelineId: string,
   370	  stage: string,
   371	): Promise<void> {
   372	  const sidecars = await readAllSidecars(projectRoot);
   373	  if (sidecars.length === 0) return;
   374	
   375	  // Lazy-load lane configs so we resolve each entry's template once.
   376	  // Importing here (rather than at the top of the module) avoids a
   377	  // load-order cycle with `lanes/operations/move.ts` which also reads
   378	  // sidecars + pipelines.
   379	  const { loadLaneConfig } = await import('../../lanes/loader.ts');
   380

     1	/**
     2	 * Editorial folio — sticky cross-page nav rendered atop every studio
     3	 * surface (dashboard, longform review, shortform, content view, scrapbook,
     4	 * help, and the studio index).
     5	 *
     6	 * Single component, every consumer. Markup intentionally flat (no
     7	 * inner wrapper) so the folio can flex its three children — wordmark,
     8	 * spine, nav — directly. The active surface is marked with a red-pencil
     9	 * underline drawn via `::after` in editorial-nav.css.
    10	 *
    11	 * Layout invariant: the folio is `position: fixed; top: 0` and other
    12	 * fixed chrome (the review surface's `.er-strip`) sits BELOW it at
    13	 * `top: var(--er-folio-h)`. Earlier versions used `position: sticky` +
    14	 * a lower z-index, which left the folio eclipsed by the longform
    15	 * review's strip — the user couldn't see the global nav at all on
    16	 * review pages.
    17	 */
    18	
    19	import { html, unsafe, type RawHtml } from './html.ts';
    20	
    21	/**
    22	 * The set of values callers can pass as the active key. The first five
    23	 * map to a nav-item that gets `class="active"`; `'longform'` is a
    24	 * special "no nav match" key for the longform review surface — it
    25	 * carries an active context (we ARE inside a review) but no nav-item
    26	 * represents that destination, so none gets highlighted. Issue 4 fixed
    27	 * the prior behaviour where the longform review highlighted the
    28	 * shortform nav-item by prefix-matching, which was misleading.
    29	 */
    30	export type ChromeActiveLink =
    31	  | 'index'
    32	  | 'dashboard'
    33	  | 'content'
    34	  | 'shortform'
    35	  | 'manual'
    36	  | 'longform';
    37	
    38	interface FolioLink {
    39	  key: Exclude<ChromeActiveLink, 'longform'>;
    40	  href: string;
    41	  label: string;
    42	}
    43	
    44	const NAV_LINKS: readonly FolioLink[] = [
    45	  { key: 'index', href: '/dev/', label: 'Index' },
    46	  { key: 'dashboard', href: '/dev/editorial-studio', label: 'Dashboard' },
    47	  { key: 'content', href: '/dev/content', label: 'Content' },
    48	  { key: 'shortform', href: '/dev/editorial-review-shortform', label: 'Shortform' },
    49	  { key: 'manual', href: '/dev/editorial-help', label: 'Manual' },
    50	];
    51	
    52	/**
    53	 * Render the folio strip. `spineLabel` is the page-specific subtitle
    54	 * shown to the right of the wordmark ("press-check", "the shape of the
    55	 * work", "longform · <slug>", etc.). When omitted the spine renders
    56	 * empty (an `aria-hidden` placeholder so the flex layout stays balanced
    57	 * across pages).
    58	 */
    59	export function renderEditorialFolio(
    60	  active: ChromeActiveLink,
    61	  spineLabel?: string,
    62	): RawHtml {
    63	  const links = NAV_LINKS.map((link) => {
    64	    const cls = link.key === active ? 'active' : '';
    65	    const aria = link.key === active ? ' aria-current="page"' : '';
    66	    return html`<a class="${cls}" href="${link.href}"${unsafe(aria)}>${link.label}</a>`;
    67	  }).join('');
    68	
    69	  const spine = spineLabel
    70	    ? html`<span class="er-folio-spine">${spineLabel}</span>`
    71	    : '<span class="er-folio-spine" aria-hidden="true"></span>';
    72	
    73	  return unsafe(html`
    74	    <header class="er-folio" role="banner">
    75	      <span class="er-folio-mark">deskwork</span>
    76	      ${unsafe(spine)}
    77	      <nav class="er-folio-nav" aria-label="Studio sections">
    78	        ${unsafe(links)}
    79	      </nav>
    80	    </header>`);
    81	}

codex
### Required-field copy builders can copy placeholder commands

Finding-ID: AUDIT-BARRAGE-codex-01
Status:     open
Severity:   medium
Surface:    `plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/lanes/lanes-page.ts:95-103,182-189`; `plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/pipelines/pipelines-page.ts:88-102,205-228`

The New Lane and New Pipeline builders render placeholders (`<id>`, `<template>`, `<path>`, `<stages>`) when required fields are empty, but the Copy handlers still copy that preview verbatim. That means an operator can click Copy on an incomplete form and paste `/deskwork:lane create <id> ...` or `/deskwork:pipeline create <id> --shape <stages>`, which is not a valid, relevant command and is especially risky if pasted into a shell.

Reasonable fix: disable the Copy button while required fields are blank or invalid, surface a short inline validation message, and keep the placeholder only as a preview shape.

### Set-locked builder advertises a CLI-refused empty lock command

Finding-ID: AUDIT-BARRAGE-codex-02
Status:     open
Severity:   medium
Surface:    `plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/pipelines/pipelines-page.ts:157-163`; `packages/studio/test/pipelines/pipelines-page-client.test.ts:214-238`

`buildSetLockedCommand` turns an empty checkbox selection into `--set-locked ""`, and the test explicitly asserts that shape. The CLI’s `splitStageList` refuses an empty comma-separated stage list, so the studio presents a command that looks like “clear all locks” but will fail when pasted.

Reasonable fix: either add a supported CLI clear-locks behavior, or make the UI refuse empty selection with an inline message instead of copying a doomed command.

### Page init is not actually idempotent

Finding-ID: AUDIT-BARRAGE-codex-03
Status:     open
Severity:   low
Surface:    `plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/lanes/lanes-page.ts:167-189,193-221,240-289,322-344,347-364`; `plugins/deskwork-studio/public/src/pipelines/pipelines-page.ts:141-174,177-231,240-267,294-347,350-367`

Both controllers describe init as idempotent, but every init path calls `addEventListener` unconditionally. A second `initLanesPage()` or `initPipelinesPage()` call on the same DOM attaches duplicate input, toggle, and copy handlers; copy buttons can write/flash twice and toggle handlers can perform redundant state changes.

Reasonable fix: add a module-level or container-level wired guard, or mark each wired element with a dataset sentinel before attaching listeners.

### Lanes and pipelines pages mark Dashboard as the current page

Finding-ID: AUDIT-BARRAGE-codex-04
Status:     open
Severity:   low
Surface:    `packages/studio/src/pages/lanes.ts:76-80`; `packages/studio/src/pages/pipelines.ts:72-75`; `packages/studio/src/pages/chrome.ts:63-67`

Both new pages call `renderEditorialFolio('dashboard', ...)`, and `renderEditorialFolio` maps that to `aria-current="page"` on the Dashboard link. On `/dev/lanes` and `/dev/pipelines`, assistive tech is told the Dashboard link is the current page, which is incorrect link semantics.

Reasonable fix: extend the folio active key set for `lanes` and `pipelines`, or pass a no-current key for these pages until they have explicit nav entries.
